National Socialist Party in Upper Austria Ceases Activities 66

Surrenders Arms to Show Submission

Leaders Vow on Their Honor

[Vienna] The National Socialist Party in Upper Austria has surrendered. Various groups of the Hitler Party have decided to cease all political activities and have disbanded the Hitler Youth and Stormtroopers and other military groups. The leaders of each National Socialist Party issued an oath to the head of the detective team, pledging on their honor to assist in dissolving the party's various groups. Throughout Upper Austria, National Socialists have surrendered to local authorities. For example, in Braunau am Inn, Hitler's hometown, and Linz, a stronghold of the National Socialist Party, the National Socialists have handed over a large number of military weapons and radio materials. However, many people fear that the National Socialists are outwardly submitting but are secretly plotting to subvert the Fatherland Front in order to cause trouble from within. Colonel Adam, the leader of the Fatherland Front, issued a declaration to the surrendered National Socialists, stating, "If you wish to join the Fatherland Front, then you must support an independent Austria that adheres to Catholicism, practices professional corporatism, and belongs to German culture. What should be noted now is whether you have changed your ideology and abandoned Hitler's theories. If you only stop using explosives and replace them with propaganda to destroy Austria, then you are merely changing your methods and not changing your political program." (Havas, 25th)

Poland Remains Silent on the Eastern European Pact 67

Warsaw Most newspapers here have refrained from commenting on the recent visit of British cabinet members to Warsaw, as the situation regarding the negotiations between Britain, France, Germany, and Russia is not yet clear. Poland does not want to make any statements in advance that would bind it. It is generally expected that Britain will propose a compromise on the issue of the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. According to a correspondent for the "Berliner Tageblatt" in London, it has been proposed to change the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact to an Eastern European Consultation Pact. This Consultation Pact could be based on non-aggression treaties between Eastern European countries. Poland has already signed non-aggression treaties with Germany and the Soviet Union. Other Eastern European countries that have not yet signed non-aggression treaties could sign them separately, and then all Eastern European countries could jointly sign a Consultation Pact, so that the various non-aggression treaties would be interconnected, thus replacing the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. (Havas, 24th)

Hitler Recounts 15 Years of Struggle on the Anniversary of the National Socialist Revolution 68

Metaphorically Describes Himself as a Motor Driving All People Forward

Urges Comrades to Strive to Achieve International Equality

Munich Celebrates at Birthplace by Hanging Flags

Munich Fifteen years ago today, after the German Revolution in the European War, the laws and regulations were in disarray, and the country was barely a country. Hitler first advocated National Socialism, and its first public congress was held in the Hofbräuhaus in Munich. At that time, the entire city was plastered with advertisements for the National Socialist Congress. About two thousand people gathered at the Hofbräuhaus to listen to Hitler's speech, but very few of them understood National Socialism. Most of them came out of curiosity, and some were enemies of the new movement. However, Hitler was skilled at rhetoric and was extremely enthusiastic. At the conclusion of the congress, the twenty-five articles of National Socialism were passed and promulgated, becoming the platform of the National Socialist Party. This was the turning point in Germany's national fortune fifteen years ago. Today, National Socialism has permeated the entire country, and the fifteenth anniversary is being celebrated throughout the country. Munich, as the birthplace of National Socialism, is celebrating even more enthusiastically. All the buildings in the city have been decorated with flags, and Hess, Hitler's right-hand man, came to the Hofbräuhaus, where Hitler first announced National Socialism fifteen years ago, to speak to the public. The main points of Hess's speech were that the mission of National Socialism is the legacy of the soldiers who sacrificed their lives for their country in the European War. During the European War, the front-line soldier Hitler was the first National Socialist to fight in the front lines. Today, the leader is also leading by example, fighting for the interests and future of the country as the first citizen. Hess paused briefly at this point, so that those who did not want to participate in the oath could leave automatically, so that the masses could swear together. The words were, "I unconditionally obey those appointed by Hitler and all his leaders. I solemnly swear." After the masses had sworn, German leader Hitler himself came to the Hofbräuhaus to speak to everyone. His speech was very long. First, he recounted the history of the National Socialist Party's fifteen years of struggle. During Hitler's speech, the audience repeatedly stood up, applauded, and cheered. Hitler said that his initiation of the National Socialist movement was not the creation of something new, but simply the awakening of good German citizens who were sleeping soundly. Hitler then briefly described the state of Germany before the November Revolution. At that time, public morality was declining day by day, and the corruption of public administration had reached its peak. Embezzlement and bribery were rampant, and the law was non-existent. The National Socialist movement did not have a strong backing, but only fought to the death with the left wing with bare hands, while the right-wing parties ridiculed and watched from the sidelines. He himself had to constantly eliminate deeply ingrained elements of doubt on the left and right. After the things he predicted gradually came true, he was gradually able to gain the trust of the people. The belief in political power cannot be solely promulgated by those in high positions, but must be gradually built up by the people's belief. Although the National Socialist Party has now seized the power of the state, its mission has not yet been completed, and its importance has not diminished. Therefore, the party is only a motor that can generate power and drive the entire country forward to complete its purpose and intention. Hitler finally requested that the old comrades continue to strive for the honor of the country and the equal rights of nations, and said that Germany should respond "yes" to calls for international cooperation to safeguard peace, but should respond "no" to arguments that deny equality. (National Telegram, 24th)

Swiss Citizens Vote to Extend Military Service Years 70

Youth Compulsory Military Training

Neutral Countries Trend Toward Nationalism

Swiss Capital The bill to extend the years of military service in Switzerland has been passed by the Federal Assembly. It has now been voted on by the citizens in a referendum according to constitutional procedure. The result was a majority of 506,845 votes to 431,902 votes in favor. Before this referendum on the bill, there was much propaganda against the bill throughout the country. The Communist Party and some members of the Socialist Party believed that aircraft would play an important role in future wars and that extending the years of military service would not be helpful, so they strongly opposed it. However, the bill was finally passed in the referendum. (Havas, 24th)

Zurich, Switzerland Today, Switzerland has passed the reorganization of the army. This case was voted on by the people of the whole country, with 485,000 votes in favor and 421,700 against. Traditionally, Switzerland has been peaceful, but according to this government order, compulsory military training for young people will also be increased, i.e., cavalry training will be increased from 92 days to 102 days, infantry training will be increased from 77 days to 88 days, and engineering training will be increased from 67 days to 88 days. Young people are required to receive military training when they reach a certain age, but no standing army is established. Therefore, what was voted on this time was to increase the period of this training. The proposal was put forward by the government and passed by Congress on September 24 last year. However, because the Socialist Party and the Communist Party strongly opposed it, the people of the whole country voted on it again. Switzerland has always adhered to neutrality, and its four million people all adhere to peace. Officials say that the increase in the number of military training days is not an expression of war, but only an increase in the technical needs of training. The people's vote in favor is also an expression of trust in the government and has no military significance. (National Telegram, 24th)

[Geneva] The bill to extend the years of military service in Switzerland was voted on by the citizens in a referendum yesterday, with a majority of more than 500,000 votes to 430,000 votes in favor. Today, the newspapers here have commented on it one after another. "The Swiss Newspaper" said that the number of votes against yesterday's vote was quite large. This is because the Swiss farmers are living in poverty and cast negative votes to express their dissatisfaction. Most farmers support the extension of the military service period, but they cast a negative vote to express their protest because they are dissatisfied with the status quo. "The Geneva Daily" believes that nationalism has won a victory, which is very gratifying. "The Labor Newspaper" of the Socialist Party said that the canton of Geneva voted in favor of the bill by a majority, which was very unexpected. Most people must be against the extension of the military service period. (Havas, 25th)

18 Japanese Fighter Planes Train in Aerial Combat 72

From March 5th to 8th

[Tokyo] A Japanese army communique said that the Kagamigahara Air Force 1st Regiment is scheduled to conduct long-distance aerial combat training from March 5th to 8th, from Kagamigahara via Tateishi and Ulsan to Gyeongseong, a distance of 2,600 kilometers. The aircraft used will be Type 91 fighters, with three aircraft forming a team, for a total of six teams of eighteen aircraft. Regiment Commander Kunino will personally command, and the purpose is threefold: (1) to train long-distance aviation technology, (2) to train in maritime operations, and (3) to train in aerial combat. The team will be equipped with night flight equipment and machine guns and plans to practice aerial combat in Tateishi. It will depart from Kagamigahara on March 5th, arrive in Tateishi on the 6th, then fly to Gyeongseong via Ulsan, arrive in Gyeongseong on the 6th, return from Gyeongseong to Tateishi on the 7th, and return to Kagamigahara on the 8th. (China United Press, 25th)

Paraguay Explains Reason for Withdrawing from League 78

Dissatisfied with League of Nations Mediation Proposals

Abuse of Power Fuels Aggression

Withdrawal Effective Two Years After Notification

[Geneva] League of Nations authorities announced today that they have received Paraguay's notification of withdrawal from the League, the reason being dissatisfaction with the League's Chaco armistice proposal. According to regulations, formal withdrawal will only take effect two years after the League receives the notification. Therefore, Paraguay is still subject to League control for now. (24th National Telegram)

[Geneva] The South American Republic of Paraguay has declared its withdrawal from the League of Nations. In a telegram to the League, it stated the reasons for its withdrawal, roughly as follows: "Paraguay did not reject the resolution passed by the League of Nations Assembly on November 24, 1934, to resolve the Chaco dispute, but requested that the main points of the resolution be reconsidered and that points conflicting with the Paraguayan constitution be removed. However, the League of Nations Chaco Incident Advisory Committee considered the Paraguayan government's request to be equivalent to rejecting the resolution and decided to adopt pre-determined sanctions. Regarding the arms embargo to the belligerent countries, Bolivia initially protested, but Paraguay acknowledged it as a legitimate measure, as it is a just action for a neutral country to exercise its sovereignty to stop the war. However, despite Paraguay's request, the League of Nations did not order an investigation into war responsibility. The Advisory Committee rescinded the resolution to embargo arms to Bolivia and imposed a unilateral arms embargo on Paraguay as retaliation. The League of Nations' abuse of power fuels the arrogance of aggressor nations, allowing them to achieve what they could not achieve with their original military force. The Advisory Committee's decision is an arbitrary action. Paraguay, as a member of the League of Nations, believes that its obligations should be limited to those specified in the Covenant and that it should enjoy equal treatment with other nations. Therefore, the Paraguayan government hereby formally notifies its withdrawal from the League of Nations." (24th Havas Telegram)

[Geneva] Paraguay's notification of withdrawal from the League of Nations has been delivered to the League today. The deadline set by the League Assembly to adopt a solution to the Chaco dispute, limited to three months, has now expired. Therefore, under the League of Nations Covenant, Bolivia is now in a state of legal war, while Paraguay's position is illegal. However, the League of Nations may not adopt extreme measures such as severing commercial and diplomatic relations with Paraguay, as stipulated in the League of Nations Covenant, as it is expected that the United States and Brazil will not approve of such measures. At the same time, there is still hope for South American countries to mediate. According to news from the capital of Paraguay today, the Paraguayan government's communication to the League of Nations stated that the League completely ignored Paraguay's request to determine responsibility for the Chaco dispute, so the League no longer has the right to impose sanctions. (24th Reuters Telegram)

Inquest Opens for Sister's Suicide by Air Case 82

Reading of Two Sisters' Tearful Wills

Court Rules Suicide Due to Derangement

[London] The inquest into the deaths of the two sisters who died in a plane crash in Essex, England, on February 21st, opened today. The coroner ruled that they committed suicide due to mental derangement. According to the testimony of the two sisters' father, the US Consul General in Naples, Mr. Bowes, the younger daughter was in love with aviation officer Mr. Forbes. After Mr. Forbes died in an airship accident, the daughter was greatly saddened. Also, according to the pilot of the plane the two sisters were in, even if he had seen the two sisters trying to jump out, he would not have been able to stop them. The coroner then read two letters left by the two sisters in the plane to their parents, stating that the two sisters were deeply in love with Mr. Forbes and aviation officer Mr. Pettie, who died with Forbes. One letter also stated that Mr. Forbes had been engaged to a certain woman, but promised to break off the engagement and marry the younger daughter this summer. One passage stated that the daughters hoped their parents would know that they would be with Forbes forever in the afterlife and that they would fulfill their promise. The sentiments were so tearful that one could not bear to finish reading them. The two sisters' father had requested that the two letters not be published, as he wished to read them with his wife and not let outsiders know. However, the coroner said that they must be read in court because they were directly related to the two sisters' deaths. He also said, "I cannot stop the newspapers from publishing them." (25th Reuters Telegram)

French Scientist Invents "Magic" Glasses 83

Made of Micro-Blue and Yellow Colored Lenses

Wearing Them Gives a Three-Dimensional Feeling When Watching Movies

[Paris] Auguste Lumière (last name), the famous physicist who is over seventy years old, has recently invented a "magic" pair of glasses, the result of which will greatly revolutionize movies. Lumière was one of the inventors of cinema. He has found two colors among one thousand five hundred colors and made lenses separately to prepare glasses. Using them to view a photo, you can see the image of the real thing and have a three-dimensional feeling. One of these lenses has a slight blue tint, through which all green, yellow, orange, and red pigments can pass. The other has a slight yellow tint, through which all green, purple, indigo, and blue pigments can pass. In this way, all the pigments in sunlight are complete. When the two lenses are mixed, the viewer only sees white, which is no different from natural light, so the eyes will not be fatigued. Lumière is scheduled to show a film taken based on the above principles at the National Academy of Sciences next Monday. All members of the Academy of Sciences will wear specially made two-color glasses. The viewing experience will be profound, because if there is a scene of a train speeding in the film, coupled with the three-dimensional feeling, it is as if it is about to jump out of the screen and rush towards the viewer. (24th Havas Telegram)

Overview of Opium Addiction in Changchun 113

Annual Sales Reach 1.5 Million Yuan

Monthly Consumption Reaches 110,000 People

Changchun Correspondence: Changchun is the location of the puppet capital and the main base of the Japanese. The opium retail stores in the city have had the highest sales of any city since they opened in April 1933. At that time, there were only about 20 businesses operating in this industry. In May of the same year, the puppet Monopoly Bureau designated another 26 stores one after another. Monthly sales were about 110,000 taels. Since then, the number of addicts has increased day by day. According to statistics from the puppet Special Municipal Government, by February of last year, the number of opium retail stores in the city had increased to 38, and monthly sales had reached more than 146,000 yuan. Sales surged around March, breaking through 290,000 yuan, the highest record of the year. Looking at the statistics, the average number of smokers per month last year was about 100,000, and the sales amount was mostly above 100,000 yuan. The number of smokers, the amount of raw opium and prepared opium sold, and the amount of money involved in each month are recorded below, so that the situation of opium consumption in the city can be seen.

Guangzhou City Maintains Municipal Bank Notes 114

Borrowing Money from Foreign Banks in Hong Kong for Redemption

Full Use of Municipal Bank Notes Restored

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Municipal Bank in this city issues municipal bank notes, divided into one yuan, five yuan, and ten yuan denominations. The credit of these notes is solid, and the citizens have always been happy to use them. Moreover, because the total amount issued is not large, and the monthly municipal tax revenue guarantees them, there have been no financial panics over the years. However, last year, the city treasury's expenditures were too large, and cash flow was not smooth. The municipal notes suddenly experienced a discount panic. The Municipal Bank owns many real estate properties, but due to the economic exhaustion of society, all properties could not be sold at once, so the municipal notes could not be maintained and were discounted to about 80%. It has been more than half a year since then. Although there has been a slight rise recently, a one-yuan municipal note is only worth 90%. The municipal authorities believed that if the municipal notes were discounted for a long time, it would inevitably lead to public and private difficulties. At the beginning of this month, they proceeded to borrow a large sum of money for the full redemption of municipal notes. At that time, special personnel were sent to Hong Kong to negotiate with a foreign bank several times to borrow money. A solution has already been negotiated and a contract can be signed soon. It is heard that the money borrowed by the Municipal Bank from a foreign bank in Hong Kong is about HK$1.3 million, equivalent to about 1.7 million Cantonese dollars. The interest is calculated according to ordinary terms, stating that the principal and interest will be repaid in six months, about 200,000 each month. The newly reclaimed land in Henan Inner Harbor is used as collateral. After this news spread, the banking industry in the city, believing that the municipal notes were maintained by a large loan, purchased the municipal notes one after another. Therefore, the municipal notes, which had been discounted to 90%, have risen back to 94% since the 18th, not far from their full value. Furthermore, the municipal government previously changed the collection of municipal tax revenue to half municipal notes and half cash in order to make up for the low discount of municipal notes. Now that the municipal notes will return to their full value, it is reasonable not to collect half notes and half cash again. It specially issued an order to the municipal tax collection agencies and subordinate units on the 19th, saying: "This government previously stipulated that all municipal agencies should temporarily collect half in silver coins and half in paper money in order to maintain finance and adapt to the environment, and it was submitted to the provincial government for approval. Now, in order to facilitate transportation, from this day on, all types of revenue from all agencies under municipal jurisdiction, where Guangdong Provincial Bank兑现券兑现券 (exchangeable notes), municipal bank notes, and silver coins are used to pay, should be accepted uniformly in order to simplify matters. In addition to reporting to the branch and issuing a notice, this order is issued for immediate compliance and for all subordinate units to comply." This order (20th).

Songjiang 115

Family Tragedy: Iron Chains Lock Up; Escape and Report

Farmer Chen Zhaolin from Yujia Alley, Qibao Town, West Shanghai, is over half a century old and has only one son, named Zhiwen, aged thirty-two. Zhiwen had already married. Zhaolin has an elder brother, Zhaogen, who has no offspring, so Zhiwen was designated as the joint heir. However, Zhiwen is by nature weak and does not engage in production, often asking his father for money to use, which aroused Zhaolin's anger. The night before last, Zhaolin and Zhaogen, taking advantage of Zhiwen being asleep, used iron chains to lock his hands and feet, confining him in a room. They also used a red-hot poker to burn his lower body, for a total of three days. Later, the clan devised a way to rescue him, and he fled to the Sixth Police Station of the town to report the crime. Police Chief Sun Shinai, after receiving the report, immediately dispatched a senior police officer to arrest Chen Zhaolin and Chen Zhaogen. Considering the case involves private torture, which is cruel and inhumane, he immediately prepared a document and forwarded it to the Songjiang County Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

The County Chamber of Commerce held an executive meeting today (the 25th), chaired by Cai Zhongyu. Matters discussed: (1) Executive Committee Member Shen Sinan proposed that this county borders Zhejiang Province, and communication between the two sides is quite convenient. Since the long-distance telephone service from Zhejiang was interrupted last year, it has been quite inconvenient. (2) The Provincial Government Secretariat urged the completion of survey forms for the banking and money industries. How should this be handled? The resolution was that Shu Baoshan would be assigned to distribute and collect the forms for the money industry, and the Chamber would distribute and collect the forms for the banking industry. (3) The county government ordered the completion of survey forms for industry, commerce, and finance. The resolution was to complete them as instructed. (4) Committee Member Sun Shaochi made a temporary motion regarding the electricity meter usage rate, which has doubled compared to before, causing significant losses for users. How should this be handled? The resolution was that the Chamber should send a letter to the electricity company stating that when re-calibrating electricity meters with doubled usage rates for users, it is necessary to invite local government and academic organizations to supervise.

Wuxi 117

Robbery and Stabbing of Elderly Woman in Southern Suburbs

Shao Ziyi, the current deputy mayor of Qingming Town, lives in Shaoxiang, near Qingming Bridge outside the South Gate, and is from a moderately well-off family. His wife, Lu, is seventy years old this year. During the New Year, his son, Xinle, held a birthday celebration for her. On the morning of the day before yesterday, four strong men suddenly came to the alley, forcibly demanding money and rice, which they received and left. At eight o'clock that evening, the four strong men suddenly frantically knocked on the Shao's door. When the door was opened, one person stood guard outside, while three others rushed in, immediately tying Lu's eyes with a black cloth and producing a letter, which roughly stated, "Our army lacks military pay and needs to borrow 2,000 yuan in silver dollars. We will send Special Agent Yang to collect it in person," and so on. When she was tied up, Mrs. Lu shouted for help, and the bandits stabbed her in the left waist with a sharp knife, penetrating several inches. Ziyi sneaked outside the door and shouted for thieves. Neighbors heard the alarm and immediately sounded gongs to alert the public. The bandits, unable to loot, fled through the door. Afterwards, Mrs. Shao's son, Shao Xinle, carried her to Puhua Hospital for treatment. Due to the severe injury and excessive bleeding, there is concern for her life.

The various tragic conditions have already been described in detail by Mr. Wang Shaohe, the representative of the disaster area. We are deeply grateful for your kind approval. Respectfully, Zhou Guren, Zhang Ganting, Guo Lanshi, Ruan Zhongzhang, and others.

Special Article

Discussing the Construction of Gan'an Salt Warehouses: Better to Build in Jiujiang and Wucheng than in Jiujiang and Hukou. 119

— Yu Shenbiao

I. Introduction

The Salt Affairs Inspection Office, in its effort to reform the national salt administration, plans to designate locations in the four provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi to construct warehouses as a permanent solution. This plan has been approved by the Ministry of Finance and is being implemented separately. The designated locations in Hunan, Hubei, and Anhui are well-suited for controlling the provinces' water and land transportation and sales, so no significant impact has occurred. However, the designation of Jiujiang and Hukou in Jiangxi Province has caused concern. The original intention of the Inspection Office was likely that both locations are gateways to Jiangxi Province, situated on the south bank of the Yangtze River. Jiujiang, with the Nanxun Railway, controls the province's land transportation hub. Hukou, with the Gan River, controls the province's shipping artery, making it convenient for both water and land transportation, benefiting both officials and the people. However, according to the majority of Jiangxi people, Jiujiang is a strategic location and the main hub for land routes, making its construction appropriate. However, Hukou is located on the edge of Jiangxi, obstructed by the dangers of Poyang Lake, which is beneficial for transporting goods into the warehouse by steamer but unfavorable for transporting goods out of the warehouse by sailboat. In the future, commercial transportation will inevitably be difficult, especially for the counties in northern Jiangxi that rely on sailboats as their primary means of transportation, making the journey circuitous and distant. It would be better to build in Wucheng, which controls the end point of all rivers in Jiangxi, historically serving as the gathering place for goods and products from the counties in northern Jiangxi, making it convenient for commercial navigation without hindering official transportation. Currently, it is reported that chambers of commerce and shipping associations in related counties are sending telegrams to the salt administration authorities, urging them to consider commercial navigation and change the original plan to build warehouses in Hukou. The future of salt administration cannot blindly follow public opinion and should be based on facts. Therefore, I have consulted historical records, examined maps, and considered what I have heard and seen to compare the advantages and disadvantages of Hukou and Wucheng, carefully weighing the future benefits and harms. I also believe that building warehouses in Wucheng would be more beneficial than building them in Hukou. Although national policies are the prerogative of the government, how dare I overstep my bounds and offer frivolous comments, inviting criticism for a commoner discussing politics? However, even humble opinions should not be disregarded by poets, and rivers should not be inferior to the sea. This humble opinion, though offered by myself, is subject to the judgment of those in power. Moreover, the Ministry of Finance's Salt Affairs Research Association has proposed to collect materials domestically for the purpose of reorganizing salt administration, so I have presented my arguments as follows. As for building warehouses in Jiujiang, which is convenient for both officials and the people, I will not elaborate further.

II. Hukou is Unsuitable for Building Salt Warehouses

To clarify this point, I will elaborate as follows:

(1) Unfavorable in terms of transportation and sales. Hukou faces the Yangtze River, and steamers can reach it directly without the risk of running aground. As the government is determined to eliminate long-standing malpractices and reduce shipping costs, it is naturally very convenient for official transportation into the warehouse. However, as it concerns national welfare and people's livelihood, the government should choose the most convenient and beneficial option while also considering commercial transportation. Moreover, Hukou warehouse salt will naturally focus on sales to the counties in northern Jiangxi. Investigations have shown that rivers flowing through Tonggu, Xiushui, Wuning, and other counties, as well as the Xiushui River passing through Yongxiu and De'an, and the Fengshui River traversing Fengxin, Jing'an, and Anyi, are mostly shallow with many shoals, and the primary means of transportation relies on sailboats. These sailboats, known as "sparrows," can only be propelled by oars and sails to reach Wucheng. It is difficult for them to brave the wind and waves and navigate the dangerous Poyang Lake. Since official transportation is limited to entering the warehouse, commercial transportation must inevitably cross Poyang Lake. The inability of sailboats to safely cross the lake is a certainty. In the future, commercial transportation in the counties of northern Jiangxi will inevitably rely on steamers to transport goods to Wucheng before they can be loaded onto sailboats. During this process of transferring from steamers to sailboats, if transshipment stations are set up along the way, it will be costly and time-consuming, and the price of salt will increase, placing a heavy burden on our people. If goods are transferred on the riverbank, the risks are high, and if misfortune occurs, commercial capital will be severely damaged. Neither option is desirable.

(2) Unfavorable in terms of terrain. Hukou is the throat of Jiangxi Province, and its strategic location is valued by military strategists. Historical records clearly describe this. Standing in the area, one can see the scars of war. After the Taiping Rebellion in the late Qing Dynasty and the army of Yuan Shikai during the early Republic, the gains and losses of Hukou determined the success or failure of military campaigns. Hukou stands tall along the river, a natural strategic location. While it may not be particularly advantageous for offense, it is truly "one man guarding the pass, ten thousand men cannot pass" for defense. In recent times, with the world situation becoming increasingly tense, statesmen are preparing for the worst. This should be taken into consideration. Salt is an essential food for the people, and its presence brings stability, while its absence leads to chaos. This is evidenced by the recent suppression of bandits, which, despite years of relentless warfare, remained ineffective. However, the implementation of a blockade policy led to the bandits' collapse. This demonstrates the importance of salt.

(3) Unfavorable in terms of warehouse base and expenses. Hukou is a small mountain town with a narrow terrain. I have been there before and found that, apart from residential houses and shops, it is difficult to find a suitable base for building a warehouse within or outside the city. Although there is some vacant land along the river, the terrain is low-lying and prone to flooding. Building a warehouse there would require land reclamation. Other areas are rocky and difficult to level. In my humble opinion, whether it involves reclaiming low-lying areas or leveling rocky areas, building a large-scale warehouse would cost no less than tens of thousands of taels of gold. At a time when the national treasury is depleted, it is not a worthwhile undertaking.

(4) Unfavorable in terms of sales. Jiujiang and Hukou are located opposite each other and both are state-owned, so there are no boundaries. This is unlike the past when merchants competed for sales. However, "everyone loves goodness." This has always been the case and is especially true today. In the future, the personnel in charge of the two warehouses may inevitably compete for superiority in performance evaluations or other matters, so it is necessary to prevent conflicts regarding sales. (To be continued)

Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Three Other Organizations Telegraph to Request Cessation of Auction of Shenxin No. 7 Factory 120

The Factory's Assets are Worth Five Million Yuan

Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation (HSBC) Intends to Auction Today

The No. 7 Factory of Shenxin Textile General Company, located at No. 468 Yangshupu Road, mortgaged two million yuan to the British-owned HSBC. Upon expiration without redemption, the bank is auctioning it off. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and three other organizations have telegraphed to request a cessation. The details are as follows:

HSBC Entrusts Auction Announcement: Lu Yishi, Moore & Co., entrusted by HSBC, announced that the bank, entrusted by the first mortgagee, will auction off 68 mu of valuable real estate located in the eastern district of the city, along with buildings constructed on the land and machinery inside the buildings, which are listed in the mortgage documents, belonging to the No. 7 Factory of Shenxin Textile Company, at 3:30 PM on the 26th in front of the bank on Beijing Road. The reserve price for this property is 2.25 million silver dollars. Offers below this amount will not be considered. The land is registered under English registers 8386, 8387, 8388, and 9654. Those who wish to inspect the title deeds and mortgage documents should contact the bank's general manager in writing. Furthermore, the buyer must pay the full price within two weeks of the auction. The highest bidder will be the buyer. If there is a dispute between two or more bidders, the auction will be immediately reopened at the bank's discretion. Once the auction is finalized, the buyer must, in addition to signing a sales contract, immediately deposit 10,000 silver dollars with the bank. If the buyer fails to fulfill the terms of the bank's auction regulations, this amount will be forfeited, and the bank will still have the right to enforce all the terms of the sales contract.

Three Organizations Telegraph to Request Cessation: (1) Respectfully to the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Industry, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Ministry of Judicial Administration in Nanjing: According to a letter from Shenxin Textile Company, the company's No. 7 Factory, with assets worth five million yuan, mortgaged two million yuan to HSBC. Upon expiration, the company was willing to pay all interest and part of the mortgage principal, but the bank refused and published an advertisement to auction it off at 3:00 PM on the 26th of this month. Our organization believes that textile factories are important industries, and since the factory's assets are worth so much and the company has agreed to pay part of the debt and all the interest, the auction should not be carried out hastily. We request you to quickly issue a telegram to stop it in order to maintain industry and protect property rights. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Municipal Local Association, respectfully. (2) Telegram to Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan, Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, and Chairman Chen of the Cotton Industry Control Committee in Nanjing: As our industry is in dire straits, we have repeatedly appealed in the past. The Shenxin No. 7 Factory in Shanghai is valued at over five million yuan. Previously, it was mortgaged to the British-owned HSBC for two million yuan. Unable to redeem it upon expiration, the bank is auctioning it off at a reserve price of 2.25 million yuan. This matter concerns the entire future of the cotton industry, and the public is terrified. We earnestly request you to devise a sound strategy to protect sovereignty and await your instructions with trepidation. The Chinese Cotton Mill Owners' Association, respectfully.

The Factory is Worth Five Million Yuan: Xin Sheng She reports that Rong Zongjing is the general manager of Shenxin Textile General Company. Its factories No. 1, 2, 5, 6, 7, 8, and 9 are all located in Shanghai, factory No. 3 is in Wuxi, and factory No. 4 is in Hankou. It is the largest textile company in China. Its No. 7 Factory is located at No. 468 Yangshupu Road, with 56,284 spindles, 134,440 thread spindles, and 449 looms, employing over 4,000 workers. The factory manager is Li Jiyao. It is currently operating day and night shifts as usual. Its total value in national currency is over five million yuan. This time, the British-owned HSBC is auctioning it off at a reserve price of 2.25 million yuan.

Foreign Banks' Economic Aggression: Raising Deposit Interest Rates 121

The Purpose is the Same as Resuming Issuance of Banknotes

Banking Industry and Others Express Preventive Opinions

Hua Dong She reports that recently, foreign banks in this city, such as HSBC, Mercantile Bank, Yokohama Specie Bank, and Bank of Taiwan, have agreed to unanimously resume the policy of issuing banknotes. HSBC was the first to implement it, and although it has only been a little over a month, the amount of banknotes circulating in the market is already several million yuan. Mercantile Bank, Bank of Taiwan, and others are also making preparations and will soon be able to issue banknotes. The purpose of their plan to resume issuing banknotes is nothing more than to absorb silver from the Chinese market and then transport it out for profit. Although the Ministry of Finance sent personnel to Shanghai to stop them, they initially refused to comply. Recently, foreign banks have decided to take further steps to absorb silver by raising the interest rates on deposits for their customers in order to attract deposits from the Chinese people. This measure has also been implemented and is a cause for concern for China's economic future. In the past, foreign banks' interest rates on deposits were extremely low, generally around one or two li. When the war in Zhejiang occurred, the Chinese people, fearing that the war would be prolonged and affect the entire domestic economy, converted their cash into deposits in foreign banks. At that time, foreign banks, due to the excessive amount of deposits, even demanded safekeeping fees. It is difficult to calculate the unexpected benefits that foreign banks gained from this abnormal phenomenon. However, since overseas silver prices have risen in recent years, foreign banks have transferred their silver reserves to Europe and America for profit, causing an unprecedented silver panic in China. The Chinese people are still trying to remedy this situation. However, foreign banks are now redoubling their efforts, using the plans to resume issuing banknotes and raise deposit interest rates to absorb China's remaining cash. The trend is likely to affect China's economic future. Although foreign banks occasionally publish inspection reports on the cash reserves for their banknotes, Chinese authorities never send personnel to participate. As for the security of customer deposits, foreign banks fundamentally refuse to join the Savings Deposit Guarantee Reserve Committee organized by the Ministry of Finance, leaving no guarantee in case of unforeseen circumstances. All Chinese people should pay close attention to the past turmoil of the Sino-French Industrial Bank. At that time, it was squeezed and ran aground. Although it was later liquidated, the impact on the Chinese people was significant. Moreover, the purpose of foreign banks resuming issuing banknotes and raising deposit interest rates is to absorb China's remaining silver. How can this be easily ignored?

Hua Dong She reports that since Hua Dong She reporters learned that HSBC and other banks are indeed planning and actively proceeding with the continued issuance of large amounts of banknotes, all sectors of society have paid close attention to it. This type of aggression is more harmful than any political force. It is now known that American-owned Citibank, British-owned Mercantile Bank, and Japanese-owned Bank of Taiwan are also preparing to issue banknotes in succession. (This matter has been brewing since the end of last year, more than three months ago.) Hua Dong She reporters inquired yesterday morning from various parties in the banking industry, the industrial sector, and economic scholars for preventive opinions. The unanimous response was that, in this critical period, there is no other way than for the people to absolutely trust the government. If we do not exchange our cash for their banknotes, then even if they gain some advantages in trade, it can be stopped by promoting domestic products. If the compatriots across the country recall the boycott movement against Yuan Shikai in the fifth year of the Republic, under the promotion of banking leader Song Hanzhang, the reputation of the Bank of China's banknotes rose steadily, leading to the current status of Chinese banks' banknotes. In fact, the reserve funds of various banks were less than half of what they are now. Under today's circumstances, the reserve funds of various Chinese banks are sufficient, so there is no need to worry. In particular, members of various bankers' associations are actively working for the country and the people. For example, during the general settlement, the China Land Reclamation Bank was rumored to be unable to redeem its banknotes due to sabotage by foreigners. Various banks continued to redeem banknotes as usual, even during the rest period of the general settlement. This proves that the reputation of Chinese banks is not as falsely claimed by those who try to undermine them. As for the saying that some related parties should request the authorities to sanction them, there are difficulties due to unequal treaties. It is better for the people to trust the government.

Registration of Foreign Rice Stopped Yesterday 122

Rice Merchants Throughout the City Supervise Each Other

Da Gong She reports that last year, several provinces in China, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi, were devastated by drought, resulting in poor harvests. In order to regulate the people's food supply and make up for the shortage of domestic food, rice merchants ordered foreign rice from Saigon and registered with the Bureau of Social Affairs for statistical purposes. The total number of foreign rice bags ordered by this city and other cities has reached more than 6.3 million bags. The Shanghai Bureau of Social Affairs, fearing that excessive foreign grain imports would not only cause silver to flow out but also cause rice prices to plummet in the future, affecting rural areas, which is of great importance, specially instructed the Bean and Rice Association and the Grain Association to stop registration uniformly from yesterday for the sake of implementing restrictions.

Drafting Punishment Measures: After the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs implemented the suspension of registration for foreign rice purchases, fearing that rice merchants would still secretly purchase it privately, it has specially formulated punishment measures. If found, the first offense will be given a warning, the second offense will be fined, and the third offense will have a portion of the total price of the ordered foreign rice confiscated for disaster relief and price stabilization. These measures are currently being drafted and will be implemented after being submitted to the municipal government for approval.

Rice Merchants Supervise Each Other: The Bean and Rice Trade Association and the Grain Trade Association of this city have held several meetings to discuss the foreign rice incident and have announced that they will no longer order it to avoid economic danger for fellow merchants and to maintain rural areas. Recently, they received an order from the Bureau of Social Affairs to uniformly suspend registration from the 25th. In order to maintain the government's prestige and protect the interests of fellow merchants, rice merchants throughout the city have begun to supervise each other from yesterday. If any fellow merchant privately orders it, they will report it to the association for sanction.

Decimal Subsidiary Coins to be Made of Nickel and Antimony; Mint Has Begun Trial Casting 123

Because Nickel and Antimony are Hard, Dishonest Merchants Cannot Counterfeit

Hundreds of Sample Coins Have Already Been Minted

China News Agency reports that the Ministry of Finance, noting the complexity of subsidiary coins in our country and the urgent need for unification, ordered the Currency System Research Committee to study decimal subsidiary coins and planned to use nickel and antimony for the coins. China News Agency reporters learned yesterday from the committee's Shanghai office that the nickel and antimony subsidiary coins have been started on trial casting by the Central Mint. The details are listed below:

Ministry of Railways Requests: In our country, the planned silver coins of single mao and double mao were originally decimal. Later, due to the proliferation of private counterfeiting in the market, the price of silver corners fell day by day, so there were fluctuations of more than twelve or thirteen corners per yuan. Recently, the Ministry of Railways also noted that the subsidiary coins in our country are complex, and the market often distinguishes between "big silver dollars" and "small silver dollars," making business slow and greatly affecting work. The same is true for industry and commerce. It specially requested the Ministry of Finance to quickly mint decimal subsidiary coins as soon as possible. The Ministry of Finance then ordered the Currency System Research Committee to plan and study in order to realize it as soon as possible. After receiving the order, the committee summoned all members to discuss it together.

Trial Casting of Sample Coins: As a result of the research, the majority of the committee members agreed that the reason for the indefinite rise and fall of the market prices of big and small silver dollars is due to private counterfeiting. Therefore, they advocated that decimal subsidiary coins should be made of nickel and antimony, which are harder than silver and require a machine with a pressure of 200 degrees to be cast, making it difficult for dishonest merchants to counterfeit. Moreover, countries such as England, America, Japan, and Germany also use this as currency. If it is still cast in silver, private counterfeiting will be unavoidable, affecting the decimal plan. Although this matter has not yet been approved by the Ministry of Finance, the committee has commissioned the Central Mint to cast a trial for research purposes. Hundreds of sample coins with different finenesses have been cast.

A Total of More Than Eighty Pieces of Bronzeware, Etc. Selected

Two British Committee Members Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Other items include ten pieces of jade, four pieces of rhinoceros horn, and one piece of silverware, all of which are very precious. This work is expected to be completed on the 26th. It will be subject to another review during the preview to ensure that it is serious. After the Crash of Pacific-Guangdong Line Aircraft No. 3 125

Damaged Plane Transported to Shanghai for Repairs

Pilot Sent to Hankou for Medical Treatment

According to Dagong News Agency, the Pacific-Guangdong line aircraft of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, which departed from Changsha Xinhe Airport at 8:50 AM on the 22nd, carrying mail to Guangzhou, crashed at noon in Yizhang County, 50 kilometers from Chenzhou. The pilot, Karen Bell, was injured. Regarding the details of the accident, Mr. Cha Zhenhu, the company's secretary, told a Dagong News Agency reporter yesterday that when Aircraft No. 3 was about to fly over the county at 12:00 on that day, a heavy fog suddenly appeared, blocking the mountain roads ahead and behind, making it impossible to discern the direction, resulting in a forced landing and crash, causing damage to the aircraft and injuries to the pilot.

Pilot Sent to Hankou: At the time of the crash, both the pilot, Karen Bell, and the radio operator, Yueyide, were on board. The pilot suffered the most severe injury to his right leg, with minor head injuries. The Hunan Provincial Highway Bureau dispatched personnel for rescue. Aircraft No. 8, which had flown from Hankou for inspection, escorted him to Hankou for medical treatment on Sunday. As for the radio operator, Yueyide, the company stated that he was not injured and is currently remaining at the crash site of Aircraft No. 3 in Yizhang County.

Damaged Plane Transported to Shanghai: The extent of the damage to Aircraft No. 3 is unknown, as the company authorities have not yet received a detailed report. According to the secretary, the damage is not expected to be too severe, otherwise the pilot would have been in mortal danger. This is indeed a fortunate turn of events. Craftsmen are currently being dispatched from the Hankou and Changsha branch stations to dismantle and transport it to Shanghai for repairs. The amount of the loss will be compensated by the company that insured the aircraft.

Representatives of the Marine Engineers Association Return to Shanghai from Beijing 130

The Ministry of Communications Fully Accepts the Removal of Seafarers Without Certificates

According to an investigation by the Marine Engineers Association into the recent accidents of various merchant ships, such as the Tongfu Wheel of the Tong'an Company, the Zhaoxing Wheel of the Zhaoxing Company, and the Taishan Wheel of the Sanbei Company, all were caused by the employment of seafarers without certificates. At the time of departure, seafarers with certificates were often used as substitutes to clear customs. Whether these seafarers without certificates have passed the examination of the Ministry of Communications and whether they are qualified in driving and marine engineering is questionable. The Marine Engineers Association has raised objections to this. For example, doctors and lawyers who have not obtained a license after passing an examination cannot perform their duties. Moreover, seafarers bear the heavy responsibility of the safety of human lives at sea. The Ministry Order has strictly stipulated the examination method. Seafarers without certificates should not be allowed to fill positions indiscriminately, causing major disasters. They should be immediately replaced.

Petition to Beijing: For the sake of learning from past mistakes, the Marine Engineers Association publicly recommended four standing members of the association to bring a petition to the capital and submit it to the Ministry of Communications, requesting to meet with Minister Zhu Jiahua to explain in detail the danger of using unlicensed seafarers on various ships and requesting the strict implementation of the Ministry Order to replace all seafarers who have not passed the examination and been issued a certificate with seafarers with certificates in the current merchant ships. Because Minister Zhu was away on official business, Secretary-General Shi Jiyin met with the representatives and considered the opinions presented by the representatives to be a matter of urgent priority for maritime safety. The petition was received, and it was agreed to forward it to the minister for approval.

Satisfactory Return to Shanghai: At the Ministry, the representatives also met with Gao Tingzi, Director of the Navigation Administration Department, and stated their intentions to Director Gao. Director Gao also agreed to talk to Minister Zhu and then implement the petition method, deciding to first order various companies to replace the seafarers without certificates of Chinese nationality with those with certificates within a certain period of time. After the seafarers of Chinese nationality have been dealt with, the seafarers of foreign nationality without certificates will be dealt with further. They will also not be allowed to fill any positions on ships. The representatives believed that they had achieved good results and were very satisfied. They left Beijing yesterday and returned to Shanghai. According to the representatives, after the implementation of this matter, accidents on ships can be reduced, which is also good news for the maritime community.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Recovers the Shanghai-Nanjing Radio Stations 134

Limited to Reporting Sea Routes and Astronomical Climate

Private Telegrams Are Not Allowed to Be Sent or Received

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's radio stations were ordered by the Ministry of Communications last winter, for the sake of unifying telecommunications, to transfer the Shanghai headquarters and the Nanjing branch to the Ministry of Communications. The call signs for sending and receiving telegrams at the two stations were also changed to XON for the Shanghai headquarters and XOO for the Nanjing branch, as ordered. The station was also ordered to submit the staff roster and all public property to the Ministry for takeover. After receiving the instructions, the company stated that its ships had a large number of telegrams directly with various seagoing vessels every day, and there were also many exchanges with coastal stations. The Nanjing station specialized in handling the reports of various ships on the Yangtze River, which was already overwhelming. In fact, it was difficult to change to management by the Ministry. The company especially explained the importance of telegram exchanges between the river and sea vessels and requested the Ministry to exempt the change to management by the Ministry in order to facilitate maritime transport and communication. The Ministry of Communications has now issued instructions that the two radio stations in Beijing and Shanghai are exempt from being taken over by the Ministry and will still be directly managed by the company. However, the call signs have been corrected as above. In the future, the two radio stations are only allowed to send and receive telegrams for the company's own ships, reporting ship routes and astronomical climate. Other private telegrams are not allowed to be sent or received.

The Shanghai Second Cotton Mill of the Shenxin Textile Company Also Announces Shutdown Due to the Depression of the Cotton Industry 135

Workers Petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau Yesterday Afternoon

The Cotton Industry Denies Seeking Instructions from Soong Tse-vung

According to the East China News Agency, the cotton industry is in a severe depression. The Shanghai Second Cotton Mill of the Shenxin Textile Company at No. 2 Yichang Road has also formally announced its shutdown. The mill was founded in the 33rd year of the Guangxu reign and reorganized and taken over by industrialist Rong Zongjing in January of the 7th year of the Republic of China, with a capital of 2.5 million taels. Rong was the manager, and Zhu Xianfang and Rong Puren were the factory directors. Zhang Fangzu was the chief engineer. There were 56,744 yarn spindles and 7,140 thread spindles, with more than 2,300 workers. It was originally scheduled to start production on February 6, but due to practical difficulties, it was postponed to the 19th and production was not started. The factory has now formally announced that workers should collect their wages. The workers feel the difficulty of this situation and convened a temporary emergency meeting at Yinxueli, Caojiadu, yesterday, deciding to organize a petitioning group and requesting the Municipal Party Department, the Social Affairs Bureau, and other relevant authorities to find ways to provide relief. It has now been decided that representatives Li Jilin, Wang Zhuping, and others, totaling about fifty people, will go to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition yesterday afternoon. As for the report that the cotton industry will visit Soong Tse-vung for instructions, it is absolutely untrue.

Xingye Trust Company Will Organize a Municipal Public Utility Banking Syndicate in This City 137

The Articles of Association Have Been Approved by the Municipal Government for Record

According to the Central News Agency, in order to complete the mission of prospering the urban area and developing public services as soon as possible, the Xingye Trust Company in this city has decided to cooperate with investment from its peers to jointly operate various franchised businesses and public utilities founded by the municipal government. It had previously drafted a general outline of a plan to accept investment from peers to establish a municipal public utility business, which had been approved by the municipal government. In order to ensure the stability of investment from peers, the company conducted in-depth research and drafted the articles of association of the municipal public utility banking syndicate, which was approved by the company's 14th board meeting and has been submitted to the municipal government for record. The articles of association are recorded as follows:

Articles of Association of the Shanghai Municipal Public Utility Banking Syndicate, Chapter 1, General Provisions, Article 1. For the purpose of developing public utilities, the Shanghai Xingye Trust Company, in accordance with the "General Outline of the Plan for Accepting Investment from Peers to Establish a Municipal Public Utility Business," invites various banks (hereinafter referred to as investors) to invest in the organization of a banking syndicate to operate the businesses listed in Chapter 2. Article 2. The name of the banking syndicate shall be determined jointly by the nature of its business and the investors. Article 3. The banking syndicate may issue bonds for the public utility it operates in bearer form, with a redemption and interest payment schedule attached, and simultaneously issue investment interest coupons to investors. Chapter 2, Business, Article 4. The business of the banking syndicate, in accordance with the "General Outline of the Plan for Accepting Investment from Peers to Establish a Municipal Public Utility Business," may be conducted, subject to the approval of the municipal government, for various public utilities of a franchised nature and for public undertakings assigned by the municipal government. Article 5. The daily affairs of the public utility shall be presided over by the Xingye Trust Company. Chapter 3, Funds, Article 6. The banking syndicate shall base its investment on the plan submitted by the board of directors of the Xingye Trust Company. Article 7. The funds required for the banking syndicate's business shall be determined according to the pre-estimated total amount stipulated in the plan. One-third of the total amount shall be borne by the Xingye Trust Company, and the remainder shall be determined by the investors. Article 8. The banking syndicate shall provide investors with the bonds and investment interest coupons stipulated in Article 3. Article 9. The assets of each business shall be used as collateral for the bond fund and shall be managed by the council of the banking syndicate. Article 10. If it is necessary to raise additional funds due to the needs of the business, the existing investors should be given priority to subscribe for additional shares. If the amount is insufficient, it may be raised separately with the decision of the council of the banking syndicate. Article 11. Later joining investors, in addition to being in the position of a second creditor for the fund collateral, shall also enjoy all the benefits of these articles of association from the date the funds are delivered. However, later joining investors may also enjoy the benefits of the first creditor if all the original investors agree. Article 12. In addition to the above articles in this chapter, if it is deemed necessary, the Xingye Trust Company may enter into a separate contract with investors, stating the conditions that must be added in fact. Chapter 4, General Meeting of Members, Article 13. Each investor in a business shall be a member of the banking syndicate for that business. Article 14. The general meeting of members shall be held once a year in February. Article 15. The council shall be produced by the general meeting of members. The production and functions of the council are described in Chapter 5. Article 16. The rights of a member shall cease at any time after the principal and interest specified in the bond redemption and interest payment schedule have been paid off. Chapter 5, Council, Article 17. The council shall consist of three to seven directors, who shall elect one chairman and two executive directors. However, one of the executive directors shall be a representative of the Xingye Trust Company. Article 18. Each investor in a business must hold a reporter and investment interest coupons for more than one-tenth of the amount of capital in order to be eligible for election as a director. However, if there are special circumstances that require changing the provisions of this article, they shall be stated in the plan described in Article 6. Article 19. The term of office of a director shall be two years and may be re-elected. All election ballots shall be registered. Article 20. The powers of the council shall be to approve all business plans, review budgets and final accounts, and audit accounts. Article 21. The council shall meet once a month. Extraordinary meetings may be convened when necessary, and shall be convened by the chairman. Article 22. The council may convene a general meeting of members in accordance with the provisions of Article 14 to report all accounts and business conditions. Article 23. The executive directors shall meet once a week. Article 24. The council may appoint several staff members, who shall be concurrently held by employees of the Xingye Trust Company and shall not be paid. Chapter 6, Responsibility, Article 25. The Xingye Trust Company shall be responsible for guaranteeing interest to investors (the guaranteed interest rate shall be agreed upon temporarily according to the nature of the business). If the business income is insufficient to pay the guaranteed interest, the Xingye Trust Company shall pay it, but if there is a surplus in the following year, the Xingye Trust Company may recover the previously advanced interest. Article 26. Investors shall not be liable for losses in business. Chapter 7, Accounting, Article 27. The accounting of each business operated by the banking syndicate shall be completely independent of the Xingye Trust Company. Article 28. The accounts of each business shall be finalized every six months, with the dates set as June 30 and December 31. Chapter 8, Profit Distribution, Article 29. In accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the General Outline of the Plan for Accepting Investment from Peers to Establish a Municipal Public Utility Business, the surplus shall be distributed as follows: (1) 60% to 70% for dividends on bonds and investment interest coupons; (2) 10% for the remuneration of the Xingye Trust Company; (3) 20% to 30% for the public reserve fund. Article 30. A certain amount should be withdrawn from the dividends in item (1) of the above article as dividends on investment interest coupons, depending on the needs of each business, but the percentage should be stipulated at the time of investment. Article 31. The dividends on interest coupons may be collected separately without being linked to bonds, but the percentage should be prorated according to the actual unredeemed capital of the original bonds. The dividends on interest coupons shall also cease at the same time when the bond principal is paid off. Article 32. When an interest coupon is transferred in registered form, the consent of the council must be obtained first and registered with the banking syndicate. Article 33. The numbers of dividends in Article 29, paragraph 1, and Article 30 shall be announced within one month after the year-end settlement each year. Article 34. The public reserve fund of each business may not be used for other purposes without the approval of the municipal government. Chapter 9, Redemption, Article 35. The method of redemption and interest payment for each public utility shall be stipulated in a table on the bonds. Article 36. The principal due for redemption shall be submitted to the custody committee for safekeeping before the deadline, in accordance with the method stipulated for each business. Article 37. The custody committee shall be organized by the council of the banking syndicate. Chapter 10, Filing, Article 38. These articles of association shall be passed by the board of directors of the Xingye Trust Company and submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government for filing to take effect. The same shall apply when amendments are made.

Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate Actively Handles Rural Loans 138

A dispatch from the Central News Agency reports that the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate, organized by the Bank of Communications, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, Kin Cheng Banking Corporation, Chekiang Industrial Bank, and the Farmers Bank of the Four Provinces, was recently established. It has set up an office on the third floor of the Bank of Communications at No. 14 The Bund and is actively engaged in rural loan work. Yesterday, the person in charge of the syndicate delivered the amended articles of association of the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate, the rules of procedure of the board of directors, and the rules of the offices in various districts to the Central News Agency for publication. The following is a transcription:

Articles of Association of the Cooperative Loan Syndicate: Article 1: This syndicate is named "China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate." Article 2: The purpose of this syndicate is to develop agriculture and serve rural society. Article 3: Anyone who agrees with the purpose of this syndicate and complies with all rules and regulations may be invited to participate with the approval of the participating banks before the start of the year. Article 4: The maximum loan amount for each year of this syndicate shall be determined by the syndicate based on the amounts assumed by each participating bank at the beginning of the year. Article 5: The loan methods of this syndicate shall be stipulated separately. Article 6: Any bank participating in this syndicate may withdraw at the end of the year if it does not wish to continue cooperation, but any loans it has already participated in that have not been recovered shall still be handled in accordance with the provisions of the stipulated loan methods. Article 7: Any bank newly joining this syndicate shall, from the date of participation, bear the agreed share and proportion of all new loans made by this syndicate. However, it shall not participate in any loans already made by this syndicate. Article 8: The loan area of this syndicate shall be divided into several districts according to actual needs and management convenience, and the board of directors shall consider the situation and plan the operations in stages. Article 9: The loan business of each district shall be handled by the board of directors designating a bank in each district from among the local branches of the participating banks to set up an office. The staff of the office shall be concurrently held by the staff of the respective branches. Article 10: The offices in each district shall be directly under the command of the board of directors to handle loan procedures, receipt and payment of funds, and other related matters. Internally and externally, they shall act in the name of the office of a certain district of the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate. Article 11: The loan interest rate of this syndicate shall be determined by the board of directors, taking into account the conditions in each region, and shall be notified to the offices in each district for compliance. Article 12: This syndicate shall establish a board of directors, composed of one director nominated by each participating bank. Its office shall be located in the Bank of Communications in Shanghai, and its rules of procedure shall be stipulated separately. Article 13: The powers of the board of directors are as follows: (1) To approve the loan methods and all rules and regulations of this syndicate; (2) To determine the loan area and organize the offices in each district; (3) To determine the loan plan for each district office; (4) To review the business conditions of each district office; (5) To audit the loan accounts of each district office; (6) To approve new participating banks; (7) To decide on other important matters. Article 14: The board of directors shall, as needed, send personnel to the offices in each district to inspect the business conditions and audit the accounts. Article 15: The board of directors shall prepare a report on the business conditions of the offices in each district and related matters on a monthly basis and send it to the participating banks for reference. Article 16: The board of directors shall hold a regular meeting once a month, with each director taking turns presiding. Extraordinary meetings may be convened in case of important matters. Article 17: The board of directors shall mutually elect two managing directors to be responsible for the business and accounting matters of this syndicate, and may appoint office staff or transfer staff from various banks to assist in the handling. Article 18: The expenses of the board of directors shall be budgeted by the managing directors at the beginning of the year and, after being approved by the board of directors, shall be borne by the participating banks in proportion to the amount of loans. Article 19: In addition to participating in the loans of this syndicate, each bank participating in this syndicate may also handle agriculture, cooperation, and loans independently, but shall refer to the local loan interest rates of this syndicate. Article 20: All matters of this syndicate shall be voted on and become effective upon the approval of a majority of the directors present at the board of directors meeting. Article 21: The rules of procedure for the board of directors and the offices in each district shall be stipulated separately. Article 22: These articles of association shall be implemented after being approved by the board of directors, and the same shall apply to any amendments.

Rules of Procedure for the Board of Directors: Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 12 of the Articles of Association of the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate. Article 2: In accordance with the provisions of Article 17 of the Articles of Association of this Syndicate, this board shall mutually elect two managing directors to be responsible for business and accounting duties. Article 3: The scope of business matters of this board is as follows: (1) Investigation of loan areas and review of loan plans; (2) Establishment of offices in each district; (3) Review of loan reports from each district and inspection of the progress of business in each district; (4) Other matters belonging to business matters. Article 4: The scope of accounting matters of this board is as follows: (1) Preparation of the budget and final accounts of this board; (2) Audit of loan accounts in each district; (3) Preparation of various statistics and account reports; (4) Other matters belonging to accounting and auditing matters. Article 5: All internal and external documents of this board shall be issued in the name of this syndicate and shall be jointly signed and issued by the two managing directors. At each meeting, the documents received and sent shall be reported with a summary. Article 6: The daily affairs of this board shall be presided over and handled by the two managing directors. Important matters shall be resolved jointly by convening meetings at any time. Article 7: This board shall hold a regular meeting once a month, with each director taking turns presiding. When important matters occur, meetings shall be convened to resolve them. The matters shall be recorded in the minutes and signed by the chairman. Article 8: When a director is unable to attend a meeting of this board due to circumstances, he must notify another director in advance to entrust him, or his designated person, as a representative, but he shall not represent two people at the same time. Article 9: If the implementation of the matters decided by this board is indeed hindered, the managing director may state the reasons and request a reconsideration. Article 10: This board shall prepare final accounts twice a year. The first half of the year shall be based on June 30 as the final accounting period, and the second half of the year shall be based on December 31 as the final accounting period. The final accounting report shall be sent to the participating banks for review. Article 11: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Articles of Association of this Syndicate and the resolutions of the board of directors. Article 12: These regulations shall be implemented after being approved by the board of directors, and the same shall apply to any amendments.

Rules of Procedure for District Offices: Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 21 of the Articles of Association of this Syndicate. Article 2: Each office shall have a director, who shall be filled by the manager of any branch of the participating banks located in the office. Article 3: Other local managers of participating banks shall be auditors of the office in that district, auditing all accounts on the spot and assisting in all loan matters. Article 4: The director shall handle the following matters under the guidance of the board of directors: (1) Investigating the cooperative situation in rural areas; (2) Investigating and reviewing various loans; (3) Handling loan procedures; (4) Inspecting the accounts of cooperative societies; (5) Supervising the use of loans and urging the repayment of loans; (6) Representing this syndicate in external negotiations, contracts, and litigation matters; (7) Managing the personnel and accounts of this office; (8) Preparing loan plans and various report forms; (9) Other matters to be handled. Article 5: The staff below the director shall be determined by the director in consultation with the board of directors, depending on the complexity of the business, and shall be responsible for investigation, guidance, and bookkeeping matters under the direction of the director. Article 6: The expenses of each district office shall be covered by half a percent of the interest income from the total loan amount for the year. Article 7: Each district office shall prepare a loan plan in advance and submit it to the board of directors for approval before implementation. If there are any changes to the plan, the board of directors shall be notified in advance and implemented only after permission has been granted. Article 8: The funds to be loaned by each district office shall be prepared in advance by the local branches of the participating banks in consultation with the local branches of the participating banks in accordance with the budget approved by the board of directors, so as to facilitate timely lending. If there is no branch in the locality, the district office shall formulate other methods with the bank. Article 9: The funds loaned by each district office shall be copied and reported to the board of directors, as well as to the local branches of the participating banks at any time, so as to facilitate the transfer of funds. Article 10: Each district office shall have the following accounts and reports: (1) Daily journal; (2) Loan sub-account; (3) Account of transactions with each bank; (4) Daily report of receipts and payments; (5) Monthly loan report; (6) Other accounts and reports. Article 11: At the end of each month, a report shall be prepared on the social affairs, business, and economic conditions of the cooperative societies that have been loaned, and shall be sent to the board of directors for review together with the monthly loan report. Article 12: If there are any matters not covered in these rules, they shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Articles of Association of this Syndicate and the resolutions of the board of directors. Article 13: These rules shall be implemented after being approved by the board of directors, and the same shall apply to any amendments.
