Moreover, the market in Hankou only sells to foreign firms for around $30. Compared to this, Hankou tung oil is actually cheaper than Zhejiang tung oil. Therefore, local markets have not heard of any foreign deals for a long time. However, the production in Zhejiang is not sufficient to supply foreign sales, so even without export channels, it is sufficient to maintain the status quo. The Hankou market has recently remained between $30.20 and $30.30, but foreign firms have only made small supplementary purchases, failing to generate interest. Furthermore, the source is not strong, and traders are not willing to short sell without significant foreign demand. Therefore, the market feels dull. Traders are selling Xiang tung oil at around $25, and southern branch oil at $24.70 to $24.80.

Page 16

Free Talk

Not a Fable 228

— Xiang Yu

I am not entirely certain if there is such a person in the world, but in my intuition, I always believe that there is someone who sits in the clouds and constructs unreal facts. Naturally, their position is lofty in the clouds. Constructing tall tales is naturally improper from a certain point of view. However, they still need to construct these unreal facts. Whether they are fools, deaf, blind, or mad is up to others to judge. As for themselves, they don't need to and disdain to argue. What they care about is the construction of unreal facts. The term "unreal" suggests that fantasy is a significant component. However, there is also reality within. Therefore, it is not entirely fantasy, nor entirely real. But the third party can also see the reality, and also see the fantasy. Of course, the fantastic part is greater than the real part, which is an open secret that does not need to be revealed.

For the constructor himself, the function of fantasy and reality is different. It is not necessary to seek complete reality! Nor is it necessary to seek complete fantasy. Therefore, fantasy and reality are equally valued. This is not something that the third party should find strange. Therefore, the constructor hates and is most unwilling to be asked: To what extent is the constructed unreal fact true, and to what extent is it illusory? In the constructor's own view, whether the constructed unreal fact is true or not is irrelevant. Legendary stories and recorded historical facts are equally welcomed. Although the purpose of the construction is different, and the target audience attracted is different, the truthfulness is not a major condition. In addition, what the constructor hates and is unwilling to be asked is: What is the basis for the constructed unreal fact, when did it happen, and where did it happen, because the basis, time, and space are also irrelevant. Humanity's past, from the very beginning, is still a mess. We are naturally trying to clarify the events of the pre-historical period. For the events after the existence of history books, there are only records of the lives of a few people, and most of the life records are still omitted. From the primitive cave dwellers to the modern us, there have been hundreds of thousands of years in the course of time, but we have nothing remarkable. Only the means of mutual slaughter, mutual killing, and mutual devouring are slightly more sophisticated. Therefore, this group of constructed unreal facts can occur in the most barbaric society of the Ximen in Africa, in the society of the Eskimos living in the Arctic Circle, in the so-called highest white material civilization, and in the so-called highest spiritual civilization of the yellow people. Although the unreal facts themselves are not very simple, their universality is consistent.

There is no society in the world that is completely idiotic, but there are many societies filled with not too few and not too many idiots. There is no society in the world that is completely deaf, but there are many societies filled with not too few and not too many deaf people. Although there is no society in the world that is completely blind, there are many societies filled with not too few and not too many blind people. There is no society in the world that is completely insane, but there are many societies filled with not too few and not too many insane people. But these people may be me, may be you, may not be me, or you, because we do not seem to be qualified enough. We are all clowns who cannot accomplish great deeds or do great evil. This is what a clown is. Most qualified people seem to be noble rather than ugly. We have the stench of nobility, but it is not very strong. So at most, we are only fit to help with odd jobs and join in the fun. There is no share for the protagonists. Even if there is a share, it is not large. What is the reason for this? This is probably because the set we play is regarded by those who think they are not foolish, not deaf, not blind, and not insane as the most useless. Just like flies dancing with lamp wicks, after working for a long time, there is not much of a plaything that is made. Of course, the flies themselves think it is no small matter. In this sense, we may be flies, our sticks may be lamp wicks, and my voice may be the voice of flies, the buzzing sound. It can be determined that it cannot resonate throughout an era. On the other hand, it can also be determined that it is the most annoying to those who are not foolish, not deaf, not blind, and not insane.

Those who are buzzing and cursing themselves for buzzing, and those who are buzzing and cursing others for buzzing, are not necessary, because buzzing is always buzzing. It is not a bad sound!

In Memory of the Gua Lu Fire 229

— Fei Er

Xiang Di wrote to me, telling me that Gua Lu was recently destroyed by fire. Regarding the disaster for my loving friends and little friends who have lived on the banks of the Gua Lu River for three years, a huge tragedy suddenly arose in my heart.

For five years, Gua Lu has been submerged in the rampant recession. Fishermen have no fish to catch, and fish prices are so worthless; the government raises tax rates, and small businessmen suffer the misfortune of bankruptcy; the children leave school one by one, and the dark iron palm immediately presses on them. …

A village city that has been established for nearly a hundred years is now finished! The fate of Chinese colonies! The fate of poor people in a recession!

I recall five years ago, when the fire spread everywhere at the beginning of the recession, I, no, we also worried about the arrival of the fire every day, but I did not expect the people of Gua Lu to survive for five years, and now they have died! For the poor people who catch fish and shrimp, for the bankrupt small businessmen, for the unemployed workers and shop assistants, and for the poor children who have dropped out of school, what way out will the world arrange for them? For my loving friends and children, when I am still groping and struggling on the dark path of life, what comfort can I give them?

Curse this world! Curse the imperialists who desperately exploit the overseas Chinese and their big bellies! Light the flames of resistance against this world! Spread the fire all over the earth!

For the oppressed poor lower-class overseas Chinese, let them raise their heads and open their eyes wide to see the disasters that are spreading all over the world! Let them explore the future path of this world from the personal pain after the disaster!

Friends, build a new path of life well! Poor little friends, my companions for three years, may you have a better destiny in another world!

I threw down my pen and sighed. From the window, I stared blankly at the bright sunset in the west as it approached.

Metropolitan Sounds 230

— TK

Trivial Talks on Historical Sketches (5) 231

— Cao Juren

I often read Zizhi Tongjian until the section about Emperor Yang of Sui traveling south to Yangzhou, and recorded:

(1) When Emperor Yang of Sui arrived in Jiangdu, his debauchery increased. More than a hundred rooms were built in the palace, each filled with supplies and beauties; each day, one room was designated as the host, and the emperor, along with Empress Xiao and his favored concubines, visited each room for banquets, with wine cups never leaving his lips.

(2) The emperor himself understood divination and fortune-telling and liked to speak the Wu dialect: he often set up wine banquets at night, looked up at the stars, and said to Empress Xiao: "There are many people outside plotting against me; but I will still be a part of the Great Wall, and you will still be Empress Shen, let's enjoy drinking together," and then he became drunk.

(3) He also once held a mirror and looked at himself, and said to Empress Xiao: "Who should chop off this fine head!" The empress asked in surprise, and the emperor laughed and said: "Nobility and cheapness, suffering and happiness, alternate with each other, what harm is there?"

(4) When the emperor heard of the rebellion, he tried to escape through the west gate; a beauty pointed him out, and school captain Linghu Xingda drew his sword and went straight forward, helping the emperor down the gate and leading him back to the sleeping palace. Qian Tong, De Kan, and others stood guard with their white knives drawn. … The emperor's beloved son, Prince Zhao Guo, the twelfth, cried bitterly by the emperor's side; Qian Tong beheaded him, and blood splattered on the emperor's thighs. The rebels wanted to kill the emperor, and the emperor said: "There is a proper way for the emperor to die, why add blades? Bring poison wine"; Wen Ju and others did not allow it, and ordered Linghu Xingda to force the emperor to sit; the emperor used his trained towel sash to strangle Xingda to death!

This tragic drama can also be written as a very hot and lively affair. We usually read history and casually flip through it, picking out the shining historical events that catch our eye. Over time, all crab eyes naturally become subjects, and there is no need to worry about being barren.

After finding the subject, we can use many methods to write it. The first one should be the paraphrase method. In Su Dongpo's poems, there is a poem called Shao Bian, "Taking Tao Yuanming's 'Returning Home' and slightly paraphrasing it to suit the rhythm and rhyme, and leaving it to Dong Yifu, so that his family servants can sing it." The poem says:

"I bent my waist for rice and abandoned my family for wine, my mouth and body are mutually burdened. Return! Who does not wish you to return? I feel that everything in the past was wrong, now it is the dew that is about to dry. The travelers point me to the way home. Children laugh and talk in front of the door; alas, the old chrysanthemums are all overgrown, and the new pines are growing old. I am now so old! But the small window can hold my knees, close the wooden door, and leaning on my staff, I watch the lonely clouds and the evening geese fly; the clouds come out unintentionally, and the birds know when to return, it was not intentional.

Alas, return home! Now I forget myself and forget the world. Relatives have no frivolous words, and there are good meanings in the qin and books. Walking on the green hills is rugged, floating on the stream is secluded, and the trickling dark valley flows with spring water. Seeing the flourishing of plants and trees, the recluse feels emotional, and my life is about to end. Thinking about how long will I be in the universe? I unknowingly wonder where I am going. I entrust my heart, who cares about going or staying? Where do immortals live? Wealth and honor are not my ambition. I only know to whistle and sing by the water and climb the mountains, and I pour wine and get drunk by myself. How can I doubt the destiny of this life? Let's go with the flow, and stop when we encounter obstacles.

Such paraphrasing of the articles of the predecessors is a writing method of historical sketches; Sima Qian's Biography of Qu Yuan and Jia Yi used this method to write Qu Yuan's Li Sao. The historical records have these two great figures and events, and the facts are known to almost every woman and child. If you want to write it into a sketch, you can only use this paraphrase method.

Letter (Part 2) 232

— Xing Wen

Although she still teaches me to forget her, she is not without emotion. She teaches me to forget her because she hopes that I will work hard for my life. She knows that in a year or two, I will fulfill her hopes. God, I am willing to love everything about myself for her sake. She will not let me down, she will never want me to forget her forever. The letter paper is as white as mutton fat jade, and the delicate handwriting carries her unique rationality. The vigorous and elegant hook and stretch can make people imagine the new plums on the Fanghe Pavilion. She is thin, and the words are also thin. The spring breeze and willow branches are thin, but there is the wisdom and fairy flavor of Xiaoxiang bamboo.

I have received many letters, and many of them are from daughters, but in my life, no letter has made me so infatuated. When I received the letter, I was still writing a very urgent and important article. After the letter arrived, the world completely changed, and the article could no longer be written. I closed myself in a small room, letting the loving and pure brilliance emanating from the letter spread throughout the room, and let me be immersed in this loving and pure light. I was not reading the letter, I was simply touring the fairyland. She wanted me to forget her, and I felt that this sentence contained infinite comfort. Her rationality, her determination, her perseverance, and her disapproval, with an emotional word, made me feel the preciousness of her asking me to forget her.

Like a melon skin boat in the vast sea, today I suddenly found myself berthed on a fairy island. The fairy island will not bully me. In a year or two, someone from the fairy island will come to welcome me. I must work hard for my life. My life has no shortcomings. My loving mother will laugh for me, and although there is no brother, my sisters will also be happy for my happiness. My many teachers and friends who love me and help me will also be happy because of the completeness of my life. I am a happy person, this letter tells me, my happiness will last forever.

The letter is in my chest, and it has now turned very warm. I put it on my cheek, and I seem to be receiving the holy mother's loving kiss. I gently recite Tang Linchuan's beautiful sentence: "But do not betray each other in our thoughts, for the road to three lifetimes is at the Peony Pavilion." Rain sounds on the twenty-first.

The Blind Fortune Teller 233

— Ding Lang

Their straw sandals have covered the deep alleys, a hundred circles, but they can't step into the door of the iron fence. There are chanting grandmothers and charitable ladies. Although this is an unfinished feudal remnant, the appearance of the West represents the era of the twentieth century! The high walls block the blind man's thoughts. The child's shoulders have made his one hand sore all day long; the child's eyes have become his vision. The "ding ding" rings, but he cannot call anyone to ask about the passing years. Is that the rustling sound of the wind? He pricks up his ears and measures what kind of call it is. He paused for a moment, and his disappointed straw sandals dragged up the dust again!

Towards Evening (7) 234

— Qu Yi

Just like this, Hu Yiyuan smoked pipe after pipe. His heart was fluttering. He forgot all the difficulties in front of him: the bank's suspension of payments, the upper line's urging of funds, the approaching Mid-Autumn Festival, the delay in insurance premiums, the coldness of the market, and the tightness of funds. Only "this thing" was real.

"Chi--" Another pipe was finished. Hu Yiyuan then temporarily pushed the pipe aside and sat up. From one side of the kang bed, he picked up a pot of hot tea. He exhaled on it twice and put down the teapot to straighten his back. He turned his head and smiled at the big belly opposite him. "How about it? Have another pipe."

The big belly straightened up. His body moved slightly. The thick black eyebrows pressed down on his eyes and lifted upwards. A wide smile cracked on his pumpkin-shaped face.

"If I have another pipe, that's fine, but--" The big belly picked up the pipe and said, "But--have you had enough?" His words revealed flattery and also revealed the timidity in his heart.

"It doesn't matter, it doesn't matter, come on," Hu Yiyuan said, bending his legs into an arch and hugging his knees with both hands. Then he slightly chanted in his mouth:

"Ascending the mountain, I asked the boy,

He said the master went to gather herbs;

Only in this mountain,

Where the clouds are deep--unknown."

As he chanted, his bare toes rose and fell in time with the rhythm. Once the big belly had filled the pipe and started to puff, circles of pale white smoke spread like clouds over the entire kang bed. Hu Yiyuan suddenly had a flash of inspiration and turned back to ask:

"What do you think, what kind of medicine did the master go to gather?--I think he must have gone to gather tobacco paste. Because the clouds are deep and unknown! Don't you think our eyes are exactly like 'where the clouds are deep and unknown'? Hahaha!" As he said this, he burst into laughter. Without waiting for the big belly to praise his clever discovery, he was already eager to praise himself.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

On Daily Life and Diet 235

— Meng Ruo

Since people have to live, they must have daily life and diet. Daily life and diet are an inevitable form of life activity in the process of people from birth to death.

Daily life and diet are nothing more than trouble. Not only are they most troublesome, but also most monotonous. For example, you get up in the morning and go to sleep at night. It's not enough to have lunch, you have to swallow dinner again. How troublesome! Today's daily life and diet are like this, and tomorrow's daily life and diet are still the same. How monotonous!

But once you get used to it, you can live in peace.

However, although daily life and diet are the same, each person's "tricks" are different from each other. Let's start with the rich. In the eyes of the poor, the rich's daily life and diet are the most comfortable. They live in Western-style houses, eat delicacies from mountains and seas, and travel by car. Isn't this comfortable enough? Those who say it is not comfortable are not content! They don't know that people's suffering is only understood by themselves. The rich's daily life and diet are indeed comfortable. But you don't think that some people are tired of sitting on sofas, their backs ache, and some people are tired of eating bird's nest, their stomachs ache, and they are crying bitterly!

The daily life and diet of the poor are completely different from those of the rich. They can sleep on the ground at the entrance of the alley, and they can eat fried dough sticks with sesame flatbread with relish! It seems that they are much happier than the rich. They have no money or accounts to settle, they sleep through the night as one day, and eat a meal as half a day. How leisurely and carefree! Maybe some rich people envy them, just like the poor envy themselves!

However, both daily life and diet are similarly troublesome and equally monotonous. God treats the world equally, probably on this point.

The Lonely Patient 236

— Zhen

It was a misty, rainy late night. Raindrops pattered against the window. As the accumulated water increased, it trickled downwards like earthworms, weaving countless earthworm avenues across the entire pane of glass. To the moaning patient, suppressing his groans, it was simply a sketch of life!

(Humans are as insignificant as earthworms, and the path of life is like the path of an earthworm. If it encounters a towering rock, it marks the end of its lifeline).

Whether the patient's lifeline had reached a point of interruption, he himself felt it was a huge question, but that towering rock had already crushed his soul. He had once used his head as a sharp axe, flashing with primitive, uncontrolled violence, to cultivate it. Although his life force had not been wasted, the melting of the rock did not proceed as he had hoped.

(Reality is built on people's excitement, and it is also destroyed by people's excitement. Look! Ahead lies a vast and boundless desolate road, where many are sacrificed as energy, and many are sacrificed as libations)!

The patient waved his hand in a daze, his head spinning along with the room. The room felt even narrower, making even breathing impossible. A pot of holly on the shelf had also withered, its color as haggard and dim as a sixteen-candlepower electric light. A dark, oppressive wardrobe seemed like a coffin, its mouth open, waiting for his corpse to fill its hungry belly. At this moment, the cold sweat on his forehead, oozing like the glass on the window, formed earthworm-like ripples. His intuition was death! Death!

After two days of illness, he could not get out of bed. A wave of heat passed, and then a wave of cold attacked, the sweat-soaked quilt pressing down on limbs that seemed about to fall apart in pain. The windows and doors were all tightly closed, and the room was filled with carbonic acid, sweat vapor, and the smell of paint from the walls, intermingling and pervading, slowly congealing his breath. His heart felt like a dried-up riverbed, cracked into tortoise-shell patterns, and he wanted to find some tea to moisten it, but there was none. If he were unconscious, he could have fortunately rested for two days. But no, he was exceptionally clear-headed, systematically playing back everything on the screen of his mind. What about the future? Pink dreams were also vividly outlined and beautiful, but now, the doors hadn't been opened for two days, he hadn't eaten for two days, and he was as desolate as sleeping in an ancient tomb!

(In this world, there are many who are rejected by happiness! Happiness adorns herself with a crowned colorful dress, with a fair face and pearly lips. This sacred virgin teases the thoughts and pursuits of countless people! Look, for her sake, many are sacrificed as energy, and many are sacrificed as libations)!

The demon of illness violently bound him, and at this moment he felt that death was the only release.

The Story of the Candle Flower 237

— Jing Jia

"Look, what a long candle flower!"

Ten-year-old Chen stood in front of the table, staring in astonishment at a large red candle on the candlestick and shouting. The other children in the room also focused their attention on the inch-long candle flower, each innocent face floating with a sweet, childlike smile.

"Where does the candle flower come from?" Six-year-old Zhen asked mysteriously.

No one could answer, and they stared blankly at each other.

"I know," after a moment of silence, the oldest, Chen, shouted triumphantly, "I know. The candle flower comes from the Bodhisattva. My mother said so."

The children were satisfied with this answer. However, a new question arose: "Why does the Bodhisattva have candle flowers growing?" This was asked by Yun, who was sitting on a small chair. Yun was an eight-year-old girl, the most beautiful of the children.

"Candle flowers are blessings. Luck." The answer was still from the oldest.

"What is a blessing?" Ling asked.

"And what is luck?" Yun asked carefully.

"Blessings and luck are the same thing," Chen replied lightly. He was competitive and eager to maintain his "knows the most" honor, so although he felt very empty inside, he still tried to remain calm.

"Then, what exactly is it?" Yun asked.

"Blessing is luck, and luck is blessing, you fool!" Chen replied loudly.

The children looked at each other in confusion. Although they were full of questions, they were afraid of Chen's loud voice, so they remained silent.

"Luck is a blessing, blessing is luck... Hey, do you understand? I don't understand!"

Page 18

The voice came from the other side of the table. Everyone turned their eyes to that side and discovered Yu, a boy slightly older than Zhen, who had not spoken at all.

"Don't understand?" Chen became a little angry, "So stupid! So, so stupid!"

Everyone fell silent again. No one wanted to be called "stupid," because the word "stupid" had already established a bad concept in their simple minds. But they couldn't prove that they weren't stupid.

"I really don't want to talk to stupid people!" Afraid that new questions would arise, Chen said these words harshly and walked out, swaying. The remaining children had long faces. But soon, everyone's attention was focused on the big red candle again.

"Look, the candle flower!"

On the Seven Seas Ocean 238

— Qin

The ship sailed out of Shantou harbor and reached Annam, Siam, and other places. In between, there was a stretch of ocean that the villagers called the Seven Seas Ocean, and they often mentioned it with tones of amazement. People from Lingnan remembered the Seven Seas Ocean from afar! Returning overseas Chinese excitedly waved their hands and talked at length: "The Seven Seas Ocean, the seawater is frighteningly black! Boundless, ah, truly boundless; the waves are as big as mountains..."

More of the people on deck were able to get up and walk around. Suddenly, someone shouted: "We've passed the Seven Seas Ocean!" The tone was so joyful: "Look, look, isn't that a mountain? We've passed the Seven Seas Ocean!"

I also tried to calm myself and shook my still dizzy head, and couldn't help but whisper inwardly: "The winds and waves of the Seven Seas Ocean are really not small!" The impression left in my mind as a child surged up with some trembling. On the Seven Seas Ocean, how much sorrow and suffering of the people of Lingnan is buried!

Recalling the Seven Seas Ocean that had just been crossed, it seemed as if the ship was still rocking, as if still under the attack of the wind and waves, and a hateful shadow immediately surged up. The few days of life on the Seven Seas Ocean weighed heavily on my heart.

This ship, called the Yuanli, a regular ship, went to Annam and was well known to all guests. Every time it sailed, it was sure to carry many new passengers to foreign lands to make a living. Among them, there were also many women going to foreign lands to find their husbands. These kinds of villagers were filled with bitter sorrow, leaving their homes and venturing to the ends of the earth. Looking at the green water of Shantou harbor was already heartbreaking, and drifting on the Seven Seas Ocean, who would not be alarmed and saddened!? How many people, after drifting across the Seven Seas Ocean, can return to their hometowns in glory; but many people, after drifting across the Seven Seas Ocean, never have any news; some are buried again and again in the giant belly of the Seven Seas Ocean.

With a heart filled with remorse and melancholy, I boarded the Yuanli in a small boat. On the noisy deck, I found a berth at random and sat down, feeling depressed.

As the ship slowly crawled out of the harbor, a burst of crying came from the bottom of the hold, increasing my troubled mood and making me uneasy. Listening to the incessant crying of the women, playing the desolate and heart-trembling folk songs, I reluctantly went down to the bottom of the hold to see. I did not dream that it was Sister-in-law Zao and several other women crying, their hair already showing some disarray, and the children and babies were also crying, looking at their mothers. The new passengers wore crying faces. The entire bottom of the hold was so dark, a desolate and unbearable sound, and my heart was so soft that I couldn't stand. Why did Sister-in-law Zao come overseas! I suddenly remembered the honest and silent Sister-in-law Zao. When I was young, I even thought Sister-in-law Zao was a widow! When I grew up, I learned that there was a Brother Zao in a foreign country who hadn't returned for more than ten years. Every time Sister-in-law Zao asked the returning guests, they could only say that Brother Zao's face was black from eating, and the rest was very vague. After guarding a living widowhood for more than ten years, without receiving any definite information, why would Sister-in-law Zao run away? And what would happen when she got to a foreign country!? At this moment, she didn't seem to recognize me, not calling me uncle as usual. Looking at her face, I was a little scared! It seemed as if I had a premonition that terrible things were about to happen. The ship gradually rocked violently, and I couldn't help but feel dizzy, so I had to run upstairs. I couldn't care about what happened to Sister-in-law Zao. Hearing people talk about the Seven Seas Ocean, the travelers' hearts became even more chaotic. The ship tossed me all day and all night, causing me to vomit non-stop. Coupled with the wind and rain, the ship was sealed, and I was as unbearable as a seriously ill person. It was on the afternoon of that day of great wind and rain that the ship was filled with various cries. A woman next to me told me that Sister-in-law Zao and another woman had jumped into the Seven Seas Ocean. My heart felt like it had been hit hard by a hammer. The ship continued to rock, and I passed the Seven Seas Ocean in a daze, unconscious. The cries and chaos in the ship, I didn't have the strength to open my eyes and look. My head was so painful, and my heart was so remorseful and depressed!

"The Seven Seas Ocean is indeed passed!" I heard someone shout, and suddenly woke up, as if waking up from a nightmare. Looking at the sea, far away, it seemed to be gradually turning green. But I still couldn't help but shout inwardly: "The Seven Seas Ocean..." In the belly of the Seven Seas Ocean, how much sorrow of the people of Lingnan is buried!

Window 239

— Hua Mu

On the south side of the bedroom, there is a four-panel casement window. Every morning, the sound of birds awakens me from my deep sleep, and this window gives me endless and far-reaching interest.

When you are silently and peacefully curled up on your pillow, facing the distant sky outside the window, and cotton-like clouds slowly drift by, your thoughts follow the changing clouds and become still, and all the suffering of the world disappears without a trace. The sky is vast and the earth is wide, with no strife or ugliness. Your whole being is dissolved in the light, plain, and tranquil beautification.

Suddenly, the posture of a hawk chasing the clouds catches your thoughts, and you will slowly have the meditation of flying. After a while, the clouds are dyed with red sunset glow, and the brilliant halo radiates over, and your cheeks seem to be dyed red as well. At this time, your heart is fluttering as if you have drunk a light amount of brandy, you think of the beautiful dreams of the night before, gently biting your lower lip, and smiling slightly.

If you move your gaze down slightly, there is a row of power lines like a five-line staff flowing across the sky to the right. Several sparrows, not knowing where they flew from, stand leisurely on the line, forming notes of high and low scales. After the wind blows slightly, the poplar leaves beat the rhythm, and simple and innocent melodies are scattered from the sparrows' mouths. You listen quietly and will no longer be annoyed by the sparrows' chatter. Everything feels round, harmonious, and lovely.

Sometimes, when your thoughts are immersed in this round and harmonious realm, suddenly, a line of black shadow flashes past like lightning, the notes on the staff are scattered, and the melody is suddenly interrupted. At this time, you will feel an endless empty silence, and your heart will be slightly disappointed.

As the sunset glow in the sky gradually disappears, this beautiful morning also quietly disappears in your disappointed mood.

In the evening, the window gives you another kind of interest. It is a faint, velvet-like light sorrow. Most of the time, it is when people are asleep and the night is quiet, and the croaking of frogs across the alley disturbs your sleep. In the light gauze tent, you look out at a corner of the sky outside the window, and the twinkling stars flash charming eyes and whisper to you. You will meditate that the corner of the deep sky is the sea, and the stars are the sea lights. When a meteor drags its afterglow and falls towards the endless end, a sense of lonely, mysterious, and ethereal feeling steals into your heart, and you will then turn your thoughts to the fleetingness of life and the vagueness of happiness. Your mood is faintly woven with a velvet-like light sadness.

In the bright moonlight of the night, when you wake up from a dream, there is a burst of light, the sky is quiet, and sparse stars are scattered in between, and there are often light silk-like clouds flickering and passing by. At this time, you are lying on a cool mat, and your thoughts are slowly caught by homesickness. You recite Li Bai's lines, "Before my bed, the bright moonlight shines, I suspect it is frost on the ground. I raise my head and gaze at the bright moon, I lower my head and think of my hometown," and your heart seems to have turned into a cloud, floating into the sky, lost in control, lost in dwelling, it is an endless ethereal, endless illusory.

So, you jump out of bed, lean against the window and face the woods and the corner of the building in front, silently lost in thought. You will hear the crickets at the foot of the wall drumming their clear and exquisite wings to praise this beautiful summer night.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

The Good Hollywood School Which Stresses the Three Aspects of Education and Imparts Intellectual Knowledge (Part 2) 243

— Zhu Jiabo

After Jimei was sent to that school for the second time, he was taken to Dr. Williams, a professor at the University of California, for a psychological examination. Then Jimei returned home with his mother to await the school's notification of whether or not he would be admitted. If his physical examination results were too far off, or if the psychological examination revealed excessive emotional instability, Jimei would have no hope of admission. However, if what Dr. William discovered was merely a spoiled child whose problems could be corrected to make him a good citizen, he would still have hope of being admitted.

On Jimei's first day at school, he spent almost the entire day in the laboratory of the head of the physical education department. The head of the physical education department was named Mark Maxwell. He used silhouette photography to capture the outlines of various parts of Jimei's body in numerous films, and then observed his physical shortcomings from those films. He also had to take footprint impressions, test the strength of his hand grip, the weight-bearing capacity of his shoulders, and the length and thickness of his legs. The shape of the top of his head, his heart and lungs, the sound of his muscle contractions, his nutrition, his skin—in short, every part of his body had to be examined in detail and compiled into various forms.

By the time the examination was completed, it was almost late at night. Mark Maxwell then gathered his three assistants and jointly drafted a physical training program for Jimei for the year. His sloping shoulders should be exercised more with pulling motions. How to gradually develop his lax muscles. His fear of pain should be given special attention in swimming and calisthenics. The next day, Jimei entered the kindergarten class. Because of California's spring-like weather all year round, the kindergarten class's lessons were conducted outdoors year-round. In the same class, he met Peter Bennett, the son of Constance Bennett, and his cousins Diana, Joan Bennett's daughter, Helen Hayes' daughter, Manford, big-mouthed Joey Brown's daughter Elizabeth, and many other celebrity children.

Jimei's teacher at this time already had a detailed report, she knew that he was overly sensitive, unsociable, destructive, bullying, and curious. She used many carefully planned games to correct the above problems one by one. She slowly instilled in him the ability to control himself, a fair attitude, and kind thoughts. His hands, which were used to destroying things, were kept busy making various earthworks and woodworking things. Soon, he found creating things interesting and completeness lovely. Later, he did not like to destroy things or tear pictures out of books.

He painlessly acquired the habit of a nap from 11:00 to 11:30. This was something he could not do at home no matter what, but at school, an hour of gymnastics every morning, from 10:00 to 11:00, had created a healthy fatigue for him, making him automatically willing to take a nap.

However, it took several months to overcome Jimei's fear of water. He initially refused to enter the swimming pool. But Mark Maxwell still made him wear a swimsuit every day and sit on the side watching many children of the same size as him splashing, laughing, and playing in the water. When he saw a girl even smaller than himself floating on the surface of the water, head down, learning the first style of crawl stroke, Jimei himself felt a little ashamed. The next day, Jimei automatically walked into the swimming pool. Mark Maxwell then patiently supported his body and taught him how to use his hands and feet. In less than a year, little Jimei could already swim from one end of the swimming pool to the other, with his head submerged in the water and his legs paddling a truly American-style crawl stroke. This kind of thing is just a glimpse of a gradual training of an elementary school student, and Jimei is just an ordinary kindergarten student.

The safety and health of the children are protected with meticulous care. Jimei's school authorities also have comprehensive arrangements for preventing kidnappers' activities for a class of children. Every student must go to the lobby of the general office before going home. There is no second exit from the entire school besides the lobby. Principal Brownt waits for them in the lobby and personally sends them to the public bus or private car. No student is allowed to leave the school alone. Whenever a student's family sends someone to pick up the student, their parents must personally introduce that person to the principal in advance before they can come to the school to pick up the student.

A year easily passed, and Jimei had already entered the first grade of elementary school. He is in the classroom every day from 9:00 a.m. to 3:00 p.m. You might think that such a long time of homework is too serious for a six-year-old child. However, he is now a burly little man who can withstand long periods of training. He is also very interested in homework. His teacher, Lucy Green, teaches him a short poem or a short speech every day, and asks him to copy and recite it himself. Often on Fridays, when all the students gather in the auditorium, she calls Jimei to stand in front of the public and recite the poem or speech. This can exercise his memory and prevent him from having self-conscious thoughts in public places. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Tear Stains" 244

— Hualun

——Carlton Cinema

After watching "Tear Stains" on the screen, one cannot help but feel a little dizzy.

War destroyed peaceful villages and scattered the families of farmers. The escaped young man, Zheng Youcheng, had no choice but to take his old mother and weak younger sister and plunge into the torrent of misery and hardship from the twists and turns of life. In the turbulent real society, one could easily sort out a theme for a script. From this unfolded work, it should have been possible to write it extremely vividly and profoundly. However, due to the confusion and superficiality of the screenwriter and director's material cutting and screen weaving, the drama they had captured was lightly let go, leaving only a pile of traces in a fleeting glimpse.

Most importantly, such as in the conversation between the mine owner and the accountant, it was not directly stated that under the foreign capital invasion, the operators of national enterprises had no way out and had to surrender to foreign forces, prolonging their lives, and after signing the contract, they could only take the road of exploiting labor. Giving the audience a deep attention to this contract from the side. Therefore, the workers' deliberations that followed could not give people a heavy feeling. And the screen let go of this light feeling, starting another stove for a lengthy scene of mining life and fainting; furthermore, the design and performance of the foreman falsely accusing Youcheng—one of the workers—of being imprisoned in order to obtain his sister as a concubine to fulfill the master's sexual desire pulled the audience hard from the labor-capital dispute to the atmosphere of how the master strongly seduced Aying, hid her, and the wife was jealous. Emphasizing Youcheng's personal revenge and the foreman's venting after being released from prison to create drama led to a conclusion that departed from the theme.

Because the original theme was determined with the life of the miners as the base point, there were more scales on the screen about the mining area. However, because the producers did not cherish the materials they selected enough and were not good at applying them, they were only used repeatedly, rigidly, superficially, and as landscape paintings. The development of the plot was neither organically linked, nor was it sufficient from the point of view of being a single screen beauty. Isn't it? In imagination and reality, the mining area should be so majestic and profound; and the life of the miners, in many films' descriptions, is so dark and bleak! But here, from the framing, angle, light, as well as the actors' actions and expressions, the appropriate flavor was not given.

Because the characters in the play do not have clear outlines and personalities, the actors are only acting superficially. Tan Ying, a female character who can act, also did not develop well. Zhao Ya does not have uninhibited enthusiasm and heroic performances. He Feiguang and Wei Helin are relatively more accomplished.

It is said that this "Tear Stains" has been cut and revised many times. Naturally, here we can only talk about what we have seen on the screen.

Review of "Marriage Agency" 245

— Jihan

Bachelor Bait - Da Shanghai Cinema

"The temptation of unmarried men," "Bachelor Bait," what a tempting title! Marriage agency, makes people imagine: there is such a house, inside there are many sex-crazed men and women, she or they need sexual comfort, she or they are waiting to get married to each other. When the cat calls on the roof, this kind of film is so tempting for some people! At the same time, we will not forget the definition of soft gentlemen's films: "Give the eyes ice cream, give the soul a sofa chair." We believe that films like this "Marriage Agency" will make them feel extremely satisfied.

In the eyes of some American writers, film is just this kind of sex-crazed thing, just like in the eyes of Chinese soft gentlemen. Sex-crazed men and women are mixed together, women must be bare-chested, men must smoke cigars and wear tuxedos, I love you I want you crazy love, the transaction of spirit and flesh, each other's bold posture, indulgence, lewdness... these become the necessary content of the film, and the playwright or director's expression of these in the work is the completion of the greatest task.

"Marriage Agency" is such a work. Here, playful dialogue is used to the fullest, and the characters in the play are selling their charms to the fullest. Cunning, frivolous, humorous, and satirical constitute this light comedy. However, we cannot find any reality here. We follow the characters in the play and laugh unconsciously. Like in a dream, walking out of the theater door, this dream disappears. This happiness is like a puff of green smoke passing before our eyes, leaving only the reality of suffering and sorrow that is tightly pressing on us.

Yes, the role of this film lies in making people temporarily enjoy and temporarily laugh. We point out that it is unrealistic. On the contrary, it makes the audience forget the cruelty of reality, which is precisely the authors' intention to whitewash peace. But the impression of "World War I" will not disappear in people's minds. For this kind of film, they only feel a bitter smile in the end.

Talking About "Marriage Agency" 246

— Guocheng

Sometimes, a person's life and hope are almost centered on the issue of marriage. Whether you are fat or thin, short or tall, young or old, poor or rich, if you do not have a good family, you will feel that your body and mind are unowned, and your life has no home.

"Marriage Agency" (Bachelor Bait) is a proof of the above facts.

This is a humorous comedy film starring Stuart Erwin, Rochelle Hudson, and Pandie Callenden.

The film depicts Stuart Erwin's journey of pursuing the truth of marriage. According to his own opinion, he said that all men and women in the world should legally become good partners. Therefore, everyone can be given an opportunity to become a useful "marriage material"; and he guides a romantic school with this theory, teaching students how to be romantic.

The business is thus unfolded, but jealous villains broke in, and things went downhill. At that time, Stuart Erwin almost lost his ideal lover.

"Marriage Agency" is directed by George Stevens and opens today at the Da Shanghai Cinema.

Film Novel

Schoolchildren's Loving Mother (Grand Old Girl) (2) 247

Lulan Belles spent a lot of time to get some evidence, and spent a lot of thought. But when she presented this evidence in court, the court, under the authorization and instigation of the powerful, did not accept her evidence, but instead rebuked Lulan Belles. Lulan had no choice but to retreat. She was thinking of ways to continue fighting with this evil force. She must find a way quickly, otherwise it would be too late.

While Lulan Belles was sitting and thinking deeply, the other party's group of people were also discussing this matter in their office. Their conversation was something Lulan Belles could imagine. Jie Lai said angrily: "This old woman is too annoying. She interferes too much." School inspector Helunte hurriedly replied: "Yes. I also feel that way." Jie Lai asked: "How long is her term of office before we can ask her to retire?" Helunte said: "According to the regulations, her term of office is still two years." Jie Lai frowned, as if he was very impatient, and said: "I'm afraid we can't wait for her to retire automatically..."

Lulan Belles stood up and went to the window of the principal's office. It was already very late, but the lights in the principal's office were not turned on yet. She stood and looked at the street outside. Across the road was Dede's place, which was brightly lit, attracting pedestrians to stop. Once the door there opened, a burst of music and sound spread out from inside. Lulan Belles' eyes had now shifted to an empty house next to Dede's place, where a "for rent" sign hung. She couldn't help but say to herself: "Clarence Dede, one day that sign will hang on your house."

The door of the principal's office opened, and a strong beam of light shone in from outside. Lulan Belles quickly turned around and saw her assistant Meilis walking in, standing in front of her and saying: "Miss Belles, it's getting late." She replied: "Yes," but her thoughts were still across the street. Meilis flipped through several pieces of paper in his hand and said: "There are a few things here..." Lulan Belles said: "Okay, please put them on my desk. After I read them tonight, I'll discuss them with you tomorrow morning." Meilis agreed and put down the things in his hand.

He walked to the door, stopped again, and murmured: "About that Dede thing, Miss Belles... I... I want you to know, I admire everything you do... I admire you for having such courage." Lulan Belles smiled and said: "Mr. Meilis, thank you." Meilis also said: "You are so devoted to the children, but they don't get any good." Lulan Belles said: "Oh, you can't blame them for that either. They go to Dede's place because that place is fun. I don't think it's drinking or gambling that tempts them to go to that place—children, liking to play and liking to be happy is their nature... and..." He didn't say any more, because a vague plan suddenly arose in her mind. Meilis suspiciously said: "Maybe that's the case. Miss Belles, is there anything else today?" Belles said: "No. See you tomorrow."

After Meilis left, her mind was thinking faster and faster, thinking about the new plan just now. She walked behind the desk, just about to sit down, when suddenly someone knocked on the door again, and three students followed in. Those three students were all particularly favored by the principal... Huade, she had helped him a lot in the debate, just like she had helped another student—that student is now the president... and William Boden, she had helped him to study the corner of Wen Zhi, so that he would not be held back, and at the same time enable him to continue the football team's work, winning the championship for the Yafangtai'er area... and Nepotong... (To be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement Architectural Weekly

New Trends in Housing Problems in 1935 248

— Xiri

Since this city was affected by the Shanghai War, according to statistics, the population of the concession has suddenly increased by more than 23%. Therefore, small residences, lane houses, and shikumen have become the target of public criticism. As soon as the topping invitation is issued, there are many people who snatch it. I have personally seen a house with no decoration, but the topping fee is as high as more than 600 yuan. From this, it can be seen that despite the tight social economy, this item of expenses still cannot be eliminated. However, there are not many people who inquire about office shops and other houses. Looking back on the real estate business in Shanghai last year, two very significant trends occurred. One is the realization of high-rise development and the gradual westward expansion of commercial and cooperative land along the Bund to places such as the Racecourse. A section in the city center, such as the new building of Guangdong Bank, the building of the Four Lines Savings Association, the steel-framed building of the Yong'an Company's expanded address, and the Daxin Company, which is being excavated, are towering high, almost like Shanghai's "Wall Street." The rest, such as apartments, with four or five floors, have been increasingly built in the northern and western districts of Shanghai. On the border of the French Concession, there are several extremely high apartment buildings of this type, which will soon be completed. According to a corner of the Public Concession, the value of this type of building has totaled 2,388,150 yuan from last year to the present; calculated as 601,600 yuan in the eastern district of Shanghai, 23,700 yuan in the northern district of Shanghai, 823,450 yuan in the central district of Shanghai, and 939,400 yuan in the western district of Shanghai. The Belgian Apartments on Kunshan Road and the Hu Si Apartments on Zha Pu Road, etc., were built in the previous two years and are not included in the statistics. The rise of this type of small and simple housing is nothing more than following the needs of the social people. Apartments with low rent and complete facilities are more and more popular among all walks of life, especially the type with two or three rooms, with rent from 75 to 100 yuan, is the most common. Among the tenants, except for a few foreigners and Japanese, most of them are Chinese tenants. For example, there is a four-story apartment in the French Concession, which has recently been completed, divided into one, two, and three rooms, etc., and it has now been fully rented, of which three-quarters are Chinese. The creation of this trend is actually because apartments are more convenient. Such as new-style equipment, rent includes heating, tap water, and miscellaneous expenses such as zero tax, making daily life gradually simplified, but convenient transportation is an even greater reason.

Our usual housing problem has always been based on lane houses and shikumen as the central premise, and we have suffered enough from various housing difficulties. Apartment-style housing is giving us a new life reform. The gradual trend of residents to apartment life, who says it is not a good phenomenon of this year.

Now, comparing the total building value of the city at 55,880,000 yuan with that of 1933, it is naturally overshadowed. However, as mentioned above, under all unfavorable conditions, construction will increase or decrease due to population relations, but the panic of social economy and the decline of commodity prices are inevitable trends! Therefore, the value in construction is also slightly lower. This cannot be said to be a decline in the entire construction of Shanghai. I remember that Professor Li Jia, the director of the French Academy of Sciences, in his speech not long ago, observed the trend of the world's population. Within the next ten years, Shanghai's population will definitely exceed Berlin, London, Moscow, and Chicago and rank third, due to its current seventh position among the world's major cities. This shows that the architectural development of Shanghai's future is just in its ascendant. We can further speculate that the construction of the Public Concession will move to the construction of the city center in the future. In fact, there is indeed a possibility. Just looking at the construction towards the city center last year is a clear proof!

Secondly, regarding Shanghai's real estate, it is also necessary for us to know about it in the past year! The golden age of Shanghai's real estate gradually declined last year. This is not due to the sharp drop in real estate prices, but because the speculators engaged in real estate transactions shifted their focus and focused on other speculations. Therefore, the amount of transactions decreased by 70% compared with 1933; it was found that the total transaction amount in eleven months of 1933 was 40,088,300 yuan, while in the same period last year, it was only 11,869,550 yuan. Now, the monthly transaction amount of eleven months last year is written below. From January to March, it was 3,753,214 yuan, of which the western district accounted for 1,400,546 yuan, the western district of Shanghai 1,335,916 yuan, the eastern district of Shanghai 401,835 yuan, the French Concession 408,917 yuan, and the city center 2,606,000 yuan. From April to May, the total amount was 2,288,000 yuan, of which the central district accounted for 1,100,000 yuan, the western district 507,000 yuan, the western district of Shanghai 266,000 yuan, the eastern district of Shanghai 117,000 yuan, and the French Concession 298,000 yuan; in June and July, because it happened to be hot weather, the total transaction amount of real estate was only 1,766,900 yuan, which, except for the 12 months during the Shanghai War, was the lowest record in the past six years, of which the French Concession accounted for 663,900 yuan, the city center 355,800 yuan, the western district 320,000 yuan, the western district of Shanghai 227,000 yuan, the central district 121,000 yuan, and the eastern district of Shanghai 79,200 yuan; The transaction in August and September increased slightly compared with the previous two months, with a total amount of 2,075,000 yuan, of which the French Concession accounted for 578,000 yuan, the central district 550,000 yuan, the western district 286,000 yuan, the western district of Shanghai 110,000 yuan, the northern district of Shanghai 48,000 yuan, the eastern district of Shanghai 44,000 yuan, and the city center 459,000 yuan; in October and November, it showed a state of withering again, with a total value of 1,976,000 yuan, of which the eastern district of Shanghai accounted for 801,700 yuan, the western district 407,800 yuan, the northern district of Shanghai 380,000 yuan, the central district 172,000 yuan, the western district of Shanghai 25,000 yuan, and the French Concession 189,500 yuan. If the transaction amount of each district in eleven months is counted, then the western district is 2,921,346 yuan, the western district of Shanghai is 1,963,916 yuan, the eastern district of Shanghai is 1,443,735 yuan, the French Concession is 2,143,717 yuan, the central district is 1,943,000 yuan, the northern district of Shanghai is 428,000 yuan, and the city center is 1,056,800 yuan. Looking at the above transaction statistics of each district, it can be understood that the real estate in the western district, the western district of Shanghai, and the eastern district of Shanghai is better than other districts. The gradual development of Shanghai's industry in recent years and the concentration of inland asset holders in Shanghai after the bankruptcy of the countryside have led to this. However, the relationship of road construction across the border is also another reason for promoting the good real estate transactions in the above three districts. Finally, this article was written hastily, of course, it is not exhaustive, and I hope readers will correct it.

Noteworthy "Courtyard" Design 249

— Pillow Wood

Indeed, the architecture of old-style Chinese houses is simple and monotonous. It doesn't possess the magnificence of foreign buildings, nor the sophistication of Western-style houses. Its shortcomings include: shallow foundations, loose structures, wasteful materials, uneven weight distribution, and so on. These have all been criticized and refuted by others. However, in the opinion of this reporter, the so-called "courtyard" in Chinese residential architecture is truly an outstanding feature of old-style buildings, unmatched by ordinary Western-style houses. It is well worth our attention and study.

It should be known that old-style Chinese houses are often counted in "advances": one advance has a main room and two side rooms; two advances have a 口-shaped "encircling enclosure." Beyond that, there are three advances, four advances, up to seven or nine advances, varying in number. Each advance generally has five bays, seven bays, nine bays, etc., differing from each other. At the very least, it must have three bays to be called an advance. Between two advances, there must be a "courtyard." The size and length of the "courtyard" vary, differing according to the terrain. Or, if there are more bays, the wide "courtyard" is divided into three to five small "courtyards" by low walls, each being different. But essentially, they are all "courtyards."

The "courtyard" is also called "heavenly well." Considering its name and pondering its meaning, one can understand that it is a blank, open-air square space in the construction of the house. The location of this kind of courtyard is roughly as described above. Its structure consists of paving the open space enclosed by walls on all four sides with stone slabs or bricks. The patterns and designs are also left to one's own preference, while the stone strips framing the edges are uniformly patterned, which is very simple. As for its effectiveness, it is quite significant: it can circulate air, allow light to penetrate, eliminating the worry of darkness and the disadvantage of stuffiness. Moreover, it is also called a "heavenly well," which can be used to dry clothes and store rainwater, making it an even better option in rural areas without running water. Indeed, in Western-style house construction, you see nothing but tall buildings, without this excellent design feature. This is an advantage for the Chinese. We may as well combine Chinese and Western styles. In places where land is cheap, if there is great construction, it is advisable to adopt the "courtyard," which is truly very convenient. However, construction must advance, and the base of the "courtyard" must be solid and even. The surface can be steel-reinforced concrete, ceramic tiles, granite, or even grass, etc., all depending on economic capacity. The aesthetic aspect must also be designed to achieve perfection.

General Situation of Shanghai's Construction in the Past Year (3) 250

— Yang Dehui

Speaking of construction in the urban area, we must first understand that in the past, urban construction wasn't particularly developed. Since the establishment of the municipal government, there had been a vigorous atmosphere, but the January 28th Incident caused it to wither again. Although the god of war is indeed terrifying, the gradual increase in population, regardless of the environment, eventually led to a gradual revival. Moreover, the municipal government's efforts to realize the Premier's Greater Shanghai Plan further stimulated urban construction, which is the main reason why urban construction showed a trend of development last year. In the six months of the previous year, the total value of construction was 12,283,000 yuan, an increase of 44 percent compared to the construction in the 22nd year of the Republic. Comparing the total value of the same period in the last three years, then, the 21st year of the Republic was 1,123,000 yuan. In the 21st year, due to the January 28th Incident, it was only 4,023,000 yuan. The 22nd year was 8,531,000 yuan. Such a rapid increase is a good sign for the future construction of the urban area. Here, the classification of construction includes 916 houses, 174 stores, 75 factories, 17 warehouses, 14 offices, 22 schools, 7 churches, 3 hospitals, and 6 other buildings. Among them, the Pudong Alcohol Distillery's construction value was the largest, about more than 400,000 yuan. The construction in July and August was worth about 4,350,000 yuan. The construction in September and October decreased slightly, but it still reached 3,431,000 yuan, including 326 houses, 69 stores, 15 factories, 9 warehouses, 3 schools, 3 offices, 2 churches, and 1 hospital. As for November and December, because there are no statistical materials at the moment, I dare not make any definitive value, but from the total construction cost in the ten months, reaching 18,927,000 yuan, the average calculation is 18,927,000 yuan per month, which is about 8,000,000 yuan more than the total of 10,841,000 yuan in the French Concession in ten months. However, compared with the total of 25,212,000 yuan in the Public Concession in the ten months, there is a difference of more than 4,000,000 yuan. This is because of the environmental relationship of the Public Concession, so in the new construction of the whole city, it can always be the first every year. As mentioned above, the construction of the Public Concession can represent the construction of Shanghai City. Because of this, the future construction of the urban area is waiting for the joint efforts of the citizens. It is gratifying to us that most of the construction in the urban area last year tended to be in the area around the central urban area, and at the same time, the junction between the western end of the Greater West District of the Public Concession (actually, there are no boundaries, but according to the current security administration), has gradually become a beautiful residential area in the past two years. The construction of Zhabei is also very developed, which is a bright sign of future revival.

Building Materials Science (3) 251

— Zhu Zhenmu

(E) Gypsum Class:

1. Overview—After mixing with water, it can harden like stone.

2. General Properties—Lighter than concrete, and its strength is also weaker.

3. Applications—Can be used as false walls and roofs.

(F) Stone Class:

1. Overview—The source of stone is all from the mountains, and its types include granite, limestone, sandstone, quartz stone, marble, etc.

2. General Properties—Highest durability, great strength, but the value is too expensive.

3. Applications—For foundations or decoration.

(G) Glass Class

1. Overview—Made from sand and other compounds by baking.

2. General Properties—Transparent, smooth.

3. Applications—Doors, windows, walls, and other parts.

(H) Paint Class:

1. Overview—The combination and preparation of various paints.

2. General Properties—Glossy, anticorrosive.

3. Applications—Protecting materials, decorating the exterior.

In addition to these two major categories, the remaining materials can be included in the discussion. (To be continued)
